<div id="page-1134109">
<h3><a name="page-1134109">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (index-page 048)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134014">
<h3><a name="page-1134014">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 001)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>1</p>
<p>Mount Auburn Cemetery</p>
<p>"The Annual Meeting of the Proprietors of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn will be held in <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, at Mercantile Hall, 16 Summer Street, on <span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1865-02-06T15:30:00'>Monday, February 6<sup>th</sup> at 3½ o'clock P.M</date>. to hear<span class='line-break'> </span>the Annual Reports and to choose Trustees for the <span class='line-break'> </span>ensuing year.  <a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a>, Secretary <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a>, <date when='1865-01-30'>Jan.y 30. 1865.</date></p>
<p>In accordance with the foregoing notification <span class='line-break'> </span>which was published seven days before the time <span class='line-break'> </span>of meeting, in several <a href='/pages/subjects/52559' title='Boston, MA'>Boston</a> newspapers, the <span class='line-break'> </span>Proprietors met at the time and place therein<span class='line-break'> </span>named. _</p>
<p>A quorum being in attendance, the President, <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Jacob Bigelow</a>, took the chair.</p>
<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/54278' title='Jewell, Harvey'>Harvey Jewell Esq<sup>r</sup></a></p>
<p>Voted that the reading of the records of the last <span class='line-break'> </span>annual meeting be dispensed with.</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> read the Annual Report of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees:  <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->The Treasurer</a> read his Annual <span class='line-break'> </span>Report, also that of <a href='/pages/subjects/55278' title='Winsor, Daniel L., Capt.'><!--Winsor-->the Superintendent</a>. _<span class='line-break'> </span>which, on motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/25008250' title='Homer, Sidney'>Sidney Homer Esq<sup>r</sup></a> were<span class='line-break'> </span>severally accepted. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134016">
<h3><a name="page-1134016">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 002)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>2</p>
<p>On motion of <a href='/pages/subjects/60332' title='Richardson, Jeffrey'>Jeffrey Richardson, Esq.</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the number of Trustees to be elected <span class='line-break'> </span>shall be the same as last year, and that <span class='line-break'> </span>a Committee of three be appointed by the Chair <span class='line-break'> </span>to receive, assort and count the votes for Trustees.</p>
<p>The Chair Appointed</p>
<p>Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/25008250' title='Homer, Sidney'>Sidney Homer</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/25008251' title='Kimball, M. Day'>M. Day Kimball</a>, and <span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/80045' title='Wetherell, John G.'>John G. Wetherell</a> _ a copy of whose report<span class='line-break'> </span>follows:</p>
<p>"The Committee appointed to receive and <span class='line-break'> </span>count respectfully report: _</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134022">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 005)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>5</p>
<p>This certifies that we have examined the books and <span class='line-break'> </span>accounts of <a href='/pages/subjects/54274' title='Bond, George William'><!--Bond-->the Treasurer</a> of the Proprietors of the Cemetery of <span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, for the year ending <date when='1864-12-31'>December 31, 1864</date>, and <span class='line-break'> </span>have found them correctly kept and properly balanced,<span class='line-break'> </span>with satisfactory vouchers for all payments charged. _</p>
<p>The Certificates of Stocks and other evidences of <span class='line-break'> </span>property were found in accordance with the statements <span class='line-break'> </span>in his accounts.</p>
<p>In the Fund for Repairs there appears to be a <span class='line-break'> </span>balance due him of six hundred and fifty four and 46/100<span class='line-break'> </span>dollars, and there is due from him in general account<span class='line-break'> </span>eighteen hundred and ninety-six 28/100 dollars.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees - Feby. 20, 1865 meeting for Organization _'> Trustees - <date when='1865-02-20'>Feby. 20, 1865</date> meeting for Organization _</span></p>
<p>The first meeting of the Trustees for<span class='line-break'> </span>organization and business was held at the <span class='line-break'> </span>office of the Corporation (33 School Street) on<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1865-02-20T10:00:00'>Monday February 20, 1865, at 10 o'clock <span class='line-break'> </span>a.m.</date></p>
<p>There were present, Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/72257' title='Adams, Paul'>Adams</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54832' title='Austin, Edward'>Austin</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Bigelow</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54833' title='Bowditch, J. Ingersoll'>Bowditch</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/62841' title='Cheever, James'>Cheever</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/65964' title='Livermore, George'>Livermore</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/70563' title='Lovejoy, Loyal'>Lovejoy</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/56312' title='Norcross, Otis'>Norcross</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/63802' title='Rand, Edward S.'>Rand</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54770' title='Read, James'><!--James-->Read</a> and <a href='/pages/subjects/65944' title='Sleeper, Jacob'>Sleeper</a>.</p>
<p>The record of the Annual meeting was<span class='line-break'> </span>read. _</p>
<p>Voted that the reading of the record of the last<span class='line-break'> </span>meeting of Trustees be dispensed with, it con<span class='line-break'></span>taining nothing requiring attention.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Ballot for Officers _'> Ballot for Officers _</span></p>
<p>The Chair appointed <a href='/pages/subjects/65964' title='Livermore, George'>Mr Livermore</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee to receive and count the votes<span class='line-break'> </span>for officers by ballot:</p>
<p>The Board then proceeded to the choice of<span class='line-break'> </span>officers: _ and the following were unanimously chosen. _</p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'>Dr Jacob Bigelow</a>, President<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ March 6, 1865. '> Trustees _ <date when='1865-03-06'>March 6, 1865</date>. </span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was<span class='line-break'> </span>held on <date when='1865-03-06T11:00:00'>Monday March 6, 1865, at 11 o'clock A.M.</date> _</p>
<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> and Messrs <a href='/pages/subjects/72257' title='Adams, Paul'>Adams</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/54832' title='Austin, Edward'>Austin</a>, ^<sup><a href='/pages/subjects/54833' title='Bowditch, J. <p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Com. to consider compensation ask further time _'> Com. to consider compensation ask further time _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Mr Little</a> for the Finance Committee requested further time<span class='line-break'> </span>to consider the subject of salaries, referred to that Committee.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Public Mont to Heroes fallen in present war _'> Public Mon<sup>t</sup> to Heroes fallen in present war _</span></p>
<p><a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->The President</a> submitted a model of a <a href='/pages/subjects/54544' title='Sphinx'>public monu<span class='line-break'></span>ment in memory of the heroes who have fallen</a> in the present<span class='line-break'> </span>war for the preservation of the Union, which he proposed<span class='line-break'> </span>should be erected in the Cemetery, to be paid for<span class='line-break'> </span>either out of the surplus funds of the Corporation, or<span class='line-break'> </span>by obtaining subscriptions for the same, as the Trustees</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134034">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 011)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>11</p>
<p>may determine.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Subject of same referred to special Comee '> Subject of same referred to special Com<sup>ee</sup> </span></p>
<p>Upon motion by <a href='/pages/subjects/54833' title='Bowditch, J. Ingersoll'>Mr Bowditch</a>,</p>
<p>Voted that the subject of erecting a monument<span class='line-break'> </span>after this model, or any monument for the purpose,<span class='line-break'> </span>be referred to a Committee of three to report upon<span class='line-break'> </span>at the next meeting: _</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>and</th> <th>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/54832' title='Austin, Edward'>Austin</a><span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Messrs</td> <td>{ <a href='/pages/subjects/56312' title='Norcross, Otis'>Norcross</a></td> </tr> <tr><td> ___</td> <td>{&amp; <a href='/pages/subjects/63802' title='Rand, Edward S.'>Rand</a></td> <td>were so chosen. _</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/53157' title='Coolidge, Austin J.'>Austin J. Coolidge</a> Secretary.</p>

<p>There were present <a href='/pages/subjects/52529' title='Bigelow, Jacob'><!--Bigelow-->the President</a> and Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='/pages/subjects/72257' title='Adams, Paul'>Adams</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54832' title='Austin, Edward'>Austin</a>, <a href='/pages/subjects/54833' title='Bowditch, J. <p><a href='/pages/subjects/54774' title='Little, Charles C.'>Mr Little</a> for the Finance Committee reported<span class='line-break'> </span>verbally on the subject of salaries referred to the Com<sup>ee</sup>: _</p>
<p>That the Committee has deemed it advisable<span class='line-break'> </span>to adopt for the regular compensation of officers the<span class='line-break'> </span>same rates as were paid last year, leaving the<span class='line-break'> </span>question of any additional compensation, which had<span class='line-break'> </span>been asked for to be passed upon this^<sup>Board</sup> in the<span class='line-break'> </span>form of gratuities.</p>
<p>The report was accepted. _</p>
<p>=== Salary of Superintend<sup>t</sup></p>
<p>It was then</p>
<p>Voted that the salary of the Superintendent be the<span class='line-break'> </span>same as last year, to wit _ <u>fifteen hundred</u> <u>dollars</u> and the<span class='line-break'> </span>use of <a href='/pages/subjects/57665' title='Superintendent&apos;s House'><!--sup-->the house</a>: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Salary of Gatekeeper _'> Salary of Gatekeeper _</span></p>
<p>That the salary of the Gatekeeper be <u>five hundred</u> dollars<span class='line-break'> </span>and the allowance of seventy five cents per week for each Sunday in<span class='line-break'> </span>which he shall Employ a substitute for the half day allowed<span class='line-break'> </span>him to be absent:</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134038">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 013)</a></h3>

<p>13</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Compensation of Treasurer _'>Compensation of Treasurer _</span></p>
<p>That the compensation of the Treasurer be<span class='line-break'> </span>the same as heretofor viz: a commission of 2½ percent<span class='line-break'> </span>on the sales of land, (not to Exceed $800 per annum,)<span class='line-break'> </span>together with ½ of one per cent on the amount of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Repair Fund: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Salary of Secretary _'>Salary of Secretary _</span></p>
<p>That the salary of the Secretary be<span class='line-break'> </span>Eight hundred dollars and the fees for making<span class='line-break'> </span>and recording instruments:</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Gratuity to Superintendt $400. '>Gratuity to Superintend<sup>t</sup> $400. </span></p>
<p>On motion by Mr Bowditch,</p>
<p>Voted that a gratuity of four hundred<span class='line-break'> </span>dollars be granted to the Superintendent in ad<span class='line-break'></span>dition to his salary for the present year: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Gratuity of $50 to Gatekeeper _'>Gratuity of $50 to Gatekeeper _</span></p>
<p>That a gratuity of fifty dollars be granted to<span class='line-break'> </span>the Gatekeeper in addition to his salary for the<span class='line-break'> </span>present year. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Question of increase of Secretary&apos;s salary Referred back to same Comee'>Question of increase of Secretary's salary Referred back to same Com<sup>ee</sup></span></p>
<p>On motion by Mr Austin,</p>
<p>Voted that the application of the Secretary<span class='line-break'> </span>for an increase of compensation be referred to the<span class='line-break'> </span>same Committee (on Finance) to report upon at the<span class='line-break'> </span>next meeting.</p>
<p>Mr Austin for the Committee to whom was referred<span class='line-break'> </span>the subject of a monument in memory of the heroes<span class='line-break'> </span>who have fallen in the present war for the preservation<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Union, read a report of which the following</p>

<div id="page-1134040">
<h3><a name="page-1134040">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 014)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>14</p>
<p>is a copy: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Comee on Monumt to Heroes _'> Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Monum<sup>t</sup> to Heroes _</span></p>
<p>"The Committee to whom was referred the<span class='line-break'> </span>subject of a monument to Soldiers &amp;c. request leave<span class='line-break'> </span>to Report:</p>
<p>That they approve of the suggestion of the President<span class='line-break'> </span>that this Corporation contribute towards the erection, at<span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn, of a monument to the brave citizens<span class='line-break'> </span>who have fallen in defence of the Laws, during the Civil War.<span class='line-break'> </span>That if the Trustees concur with the Committee, then they<span class='line-break'> </span>would suggest, that, in addition to the model already before<span class='line-break'> </span>them, Artists be invited to send in designs for the inspection<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Board.</p>
<p>Respectfully submitted<span class='line-break'> </span>Edward Austin for the Com<sup>ee</sup></p>
<p>On motion of Mr Little,<span class='line-break'> </span>The report was accepted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Comee on Mont to Heroes author-ized to invite designs by different Artists _'> Com<sup>ee</sup> on Mon<sup>t</sup> to Heroes author-ized to invite designs by different Artists _</span></p>
<p>On motion by Mr Cheever,<span class='line-break'> </span>Voted to refer the whole subject back to<span class='line-break'> </span>the same Committee with power to invite designs and<span class='line-break'> </span>report thereon to this Board:</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Reps of Lots '> Rep<sup>s</sup> of Lots </span></p>
<p>Representatives for lots were designated as follows: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 215 '> 215 </span></p>
<p>Lucy N. Goodwin of Boston, widow of Ozias Goodwin late proprietor<span class='line-break'> </span>of lot numbered 215 to represent that lot: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 1817 '> 1817 </span></p>
<p>Catherine B. Goodall of Boston daughter of Catherine Phinney, dec<sup>d</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>late prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 1817 to represent said lot. _</p>
<p>Adjourned Attest Austin J. Coolidge, Secy</p>

<div id="page-1134042">
<h3><a name="page-1134042">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 015)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>15</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees May 1, 1865 '> Trustees May 1, 1865 </span></p>
<p>The Trustees held their monthly meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>on Monday May 1, 1865, at 11 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President and Messrs Austin,<span class='line-break'> </span>Bowditch, Little, Livermore, Lovejoy, Norcross, Rand<span class='line-break'> </span>and Reed.</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' By-laws reported in a new draft. '> By-laws reported in a new draft. </span></p>
<p>Mr Norcross for the Committee on the revision of the<span class='line-break'> </span>By-laws reported _ submitting the same with alterations<span class='line-break'> </span>and additions in a new draft:</p>
<p>Upon which it was</p>
<p>Voted that the same be printed, and a copy<span class='line-break'> </span>be sent to each of the Trustees in season for consider<span class='line-break'></span>ation of the next meeting of this Board. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Com. on Public Mont ask further time _'> Com. on Public Mon<sup>t</sup> ask further time _</span></p>
<p>Mr Austin for the Committee chosen to invite designs<span class='line-break'> </span>for the public monument for the heroes who have fallen in the<span class='line-break'> </span>present war asked further time to report in form. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Conditional appropriation for Public Monument _'> Conditional appropriation for Public Monument _</span></p>
<p>Mr Rand submitted the following motion, to which under the<span class='line-break'> </span>rule lies over until the next meeting:</p>
<p>"That the Trustees will appropriate from the funds of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Corporation one half the amount necessary for the erection of<span class='line-break'> </span>a monument to the memory of the brave soldiers who have died<span class='line-break'> </span>in the war, provided such half part shall not exceed<span class='line-break'> </span>$(15,000) fifteen thousand dollars, and provided also the remain<span class='line-break'></span>ing one half shall be subscribed and paid by other parties.</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held on Monday, June 5<sup>th</sup> 1865, at 11 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m. _</p>

<p>On motion by Mr Read,</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134052">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 020)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>20</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees Aug. 7, 1865. '> Trustees Aug. 7, 1865. </span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held on Monday August 7<sup>th</sup> 1865, at<span class='line-break'> </span>11 O'clock a.m. _</p>
<p>There were present, the President, Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span>Adams, Austin, Cheever, Read and Sleeper.</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Question as to Interments of Removals from Old Bury-ing Ground at reduced price _ '> Question as to Interments of Removals from Old Bury-ing Ground at reduced price _ </span></p>
<p>A communication was received from the<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent stating that application had been<span class='line-break'> </span>made to him by the mayor of Cambridge to<span class='line-break'> </span>know whether the Trustees would receive and<span class='line-break'> </span>authorize the interment of about one hundred<span class='line-break'> </span>and fifty bodies from the Old Burial Ground in<span class='line-break'> </span>Cambridge port at any less rate of charge than the<span class='line-break'> </span>regular fee for interment.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' referred to a Comee '> referred to a Com<sup>ee</sup> </span></p>
<p>Voted that the subject be referred to a<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee of two consisting of Messrs Adams<span class='line-break'> </span>and Cheever with full power to act in<span class='line-break'> </span>the premises as they see fit.</p>

<div id="page-1134058">
<h3><a name="page-1134058">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 023)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>23</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' [Resolutions of respect to Mr Livermore to] be prepared by the Prest _'> [Resolutions of respect to Mr Livermore to] be prepared by the Pres<sup>t</sup> _</span></p>
<p>Mr Livermore, and forward a copy of the <span class='line-break'> </span>same to the family of the deceased, and<span class='line-break'> </span>that the Resolutions be entered upon the<span class='line-break'> </span>records of the Trustees.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Attest Austin J. Coolidge, Sec.y</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>----------------------</p>
<p>In accordance with the vote of September 4<sup>th</sup>,<span class='line-break'> </span>a letter was prepared by the President and<span class='line-break'> </span>sent to the family of Mr Livermore of which the<span class='line-break'> </span>following is a true copy: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Resolutions respecting  Livermore deceased, a member of this Board. '> Resolutions respecting  Livermore deceased, a member of this Board. </span></p>
<p>"Resolved _</p>
<p>That the Trustees of the Cemetery of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn feel with deep sorrow the loss of their<span class='line-break'> </span>friend and cherished associate, Mr George<span class='line-break'> </span>Livermore.</p>
<p>They appreciate and gratefully remem<span class='line-break'></span>ber the promptitude with which he entered<span class='line-break'> </span>on the duties belonging to his position as a <span class='line-break'> </span>member of their board. They have felt the<span class='line-break'> </span>influence of his kind and courteous manners,<span class='line-break'> </span>the modest and friendly bearing which tempered<span class='line-break'> </span>the outspoken honesty of his opinions. They have<span class='line-break'> </span>recognized and honored the position in our com<span class='line-break'></span>munity which he had taken by his unsullied<span class='line-break'> </span>integrity, his active and successful control of an<span class='line-break'> </span>Exclusive business, : and the untiring energy of char<span class='line-break'></span>acter, which in the midst of arduous practical</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134060">
<h3><a name="page-1134060">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 024)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>24</p>
<p>duties, gave him time to cultivate a refined taste<span class='line-break'> </span>and to deserve the literary honors which from time<span class='line-break'> </span>to time were bestowed upon him.</p>
<p>He has died<span class='line-break'> </span>as it were prematurely, in the prime of an efficient<span class='line-break'> </span>and intellectual life, when he was looking forward,<span class='line-break'> </span>apparently not without reason, to the future enjoyment<span class='line-break'> </span>of his ample library, his cultivated friends, his self<span class='line-break'></span>made fortune and the social responsibilities which<span class='line-break'> </span>he ever freely met and faithfully fulfilled.</p>
<p>The Trustees tender to his afflicted family the<span class='line-break'> </span>assurance of their deepest sympathy in this their<span class='line-break'> </span>great and mutual loss.</p>
<p>(signed) Jacob Bigelow,<span class='line-break'> </span>President</p>
<p>Attest ,, Austin J. Coolidge Sec.y</p>
<p>--------------</p>

<p>"The Committee to which was referred<span class='line-break'> </span>the revision of the By laws and the printing of<span class='line-break'> </span>the same in connection with a new edition of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Catalogue (Feby. 20, 1865) beg leave to Report:</p>
<p>That the preparation of a new catalogue<span class='line-break'> </span>has progressed nearly to completion, and they<span class='line-break'> </span>also learn that the new lithographic map<span class='line-break'> </span>ordered by this Board is nearly finished.</p>
<p>As it is very desirable that the two works<span class='line-break'> </span>should appear and be distributed simultan<span class='line-break'></span>eously, your Committee recommend that<span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees appropriate a sum not exceeding<span class='line-break'> </span>($2350) twenty three hundred and fifty dollars<span class='line-break'> </span>for the following purposes: _</p>

<p>The motion submitted at the last meeting,<span class='line-break'> </span>authorizing the Committee on the Catalogue to<span class='line-break'> </span>expend a sum not exceeding twenty three hun<span class='line-break'></span>dred^<sup>&amp; fifty</sup> dollars for the printing and distribution<span class='line-break'> </span>of forty five hundred copies each of the cata<span class='line-break'></span>logue and plan came up first in order. _<span class='line-break'> </span>and the motion for such appropriation was<span class='line-break'> </span>adopted.</p>

<div id="page-1134072">
<h3><a name="page-1134072">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 030)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>30</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees Decemr 4, 1865 '> Trustees Decem<sup>r</sup> 4, 1865 </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Comee to nominate a Gate Keeper with power of temporary appointment. '> Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> to nominate a Gate Keeper with power of temporary appointment. </span></p>
<p>The Committee to which was referred the nom<span class='line-break'></span>ination &amp;c of a Gatekeeper submitted their<span class='line-break'> </span>Report: _</p>
<p>"The Committee appointed to select a Gate<span class='line-break'></span>keeper and temporarily to appoint one beg leave <span class='line-break'> </span>to report that having examined the different<span class='line-break'> </span>applications for that office and seen the several<span class='line-break'> </span>applicants, - upon a full consideration of the recom<span class='line-break'></span>mendations presented, and personal inquiries<span class='line-break'> </span>made they have appointed temporarily<span class='line-break'> </span>George P. Southack,<span class='line-break'> </span>a  returned and wounded soldier, whom they also<span class='line-break'> </span>recommend for appointment by the Trustees as per<span class='line-break'></span>manent Gatekeeper.</p>
<p>Mr Southack, as they have been informed, was<span class='line-break'> </span>an Orderly Sergeant in the 2<sup>d</sup> Mass. Reg<sup>t</sup> of Infantry,<span class='line-break'> </span>was wounded in the arm and discharged _ again<span class='line-break'> </span>enlisted in the 61<sup>st</sup> Mass. Infantry and remained<span class='line-break'> </span>in service until the Regiment was mustered out in July<span class='line-break'> </span>last. He has since then been employed for a part of<span class='line-break'> </span>the time in the office of the Adjutant Gen<sup>l</sup> as Clerk, but has<span class='line-break'> </span>recently been discharged, there being no further occasion<span class='line-break'> </span>for so large a number of Clerks. He is married, and, as<span class='line-break'> </span>he states, has no property or means of support. The<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee feeling that a soldier who has served so faith<span class='line-break'></span>fully during the war and had been wounded in<span class='line-break'> </span>such a manner as to disable him from returning<span class='line-break'> </span>to his former occupation _ that of a Pianoforte tuner _<span class='line-break'> </span>is more deserving of the consideration of the Trustees,<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134074">
<h3><a name="page-1134074">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 031)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>31</p>
<p>than any other person can be, respectfully<span class='line-break'> </span>recommend his appointment.</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>For the Committee</th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>Edward S. Rand,,</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>The foregoing report was accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Gatekeeper chosen _ '> Gatekeeper chosen _ </span></p>
<p>It was then</p>
<p>Voted that George P. Southack<span class='line-break'> </span>be chosen Gatekeeper.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Soldiers&apos; monument _ action deferred _'> Soldiers' monument _ action deferred _</span></p>
<p>The subject of a Soldiers' monument was<span class='line-break'> </span>brought up, but the Committee were not pre<span class='line-break'></span>pared to report; and it was</p>
<p>Voted to defer all action in relation to<span class='line-break'> </span>the same until the next meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Question of enclosing Stone Farm - '> Question of enclosing Stone Farm - </span></p>
<p>Voted that a Committee of three be appoint<span class='line-break'></span>ed to consider the Expediency of enclosing the<span class='line-break'> </span>Stone Farm with an Iron Fence on the road,<span class='line-break'> </span>to make inquiries, obtain estimates and report<span class='line-break'> </span>at a future meeting:<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>and</th> <th>___</th> <th>{ Cheever<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>Messrs</td> <td>{ Bowditch &amp;</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>{Lovejoy</td> <td>were appointed.</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Representation of Lot no. 583 '> Representation of Lot no. 583 </span></p>
<p>Upon the petition of the children heirs of Levi Bartlett,<span class='line-break'> </span>deceased, late proprietor of lot numbered 583, Henry C.<span class='line-break'> </span>Angell, of Boston, son-in law, was designated to represent said lot.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134076">
<h3><a name="page-1134076">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 032)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>32</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Application of Jas. C. Merrill to reconvey his lot no. 3487, &amp; to receive two deeds of same _ referred to Mr Bowditch _'> Application of Jas. C. Merrill to reconvey his lot no. 3487, &amp; to receive two deeds of same _ referred to Mr Bowditch _</span></p>
<p>Mr Bowditch presented the written request,<span class='line-break'> </span>of James C. Merrill Esq. proprietor of lot num<span class='line-break'></span>bered 3487 stating that he purchased said<span class='line-break'> </span>lot upon the erroneous information _ or at least upon<span class='line-break'> </span>the erroneous inference from certain information _ that<span class='line-break'> </span>if the whole should prove larger than he desired,<span class='line-break'> </span>he could convey a portion of it to another; that having<span class='line-break'> </span>entered into the purchase of it with Mr Henry V. Ward,<span class='line-break'> </span>he had ascertained that he could not convey to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span>Ward one half as a distinct interest, unless so<span class='line-break'> </span>authorized by the Trustees and he asked that<span class='line-break'> </span>he might reconvey his lot to the Corporation and<span class='line-break'> </span>that two deeds might issue to himself and Mr Ward.</p>
<p>Voted that the subject be referred to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span>Bowditch with full power: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='  Letter of John T. Heard containing extract of will of Eliz. F. Gurney respecting her tomb _ lot no. 815. '>  Letter of John T. Heard containing extract of will of Eliz. F. Gurney respecting her tomb _ lot no. 815. </span></p>
<p>A communication was received from John<span class='line-break'> </span>T. Heard Esq. a copy of which follows, and it was<span class='line-break'> </span>voted to extend the same upon the records.</p>
<p>Boston, November 20<sup>th</sup> 1865</p>
<p>Dear Sir:</p>
<p>I beg to call the attention of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees of Mount Auburn Cemetery to the following<span class='line-break'> </span>extract from the will of the late Mrs. E.F. Gurney,<span class='line-break'> </span>as it provided for keeping in repair her burial lot<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Cemetery under their charge:</p>
<p>"30. I give and devise to the Trustees of the Newton<span class='line-break'> </span>"Theological Institution, all that parcel of land with</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134078">
<h3><a name="page-1134078">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 033)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>33</p>
<p>"the buildings thereon, situate at the Northerly part<span class='line-break'> </span>"of said Boston, bounded southerly by Prince street,<span class='line-break'> </span>"northerly by Salem street, northeasterly by land now<span class='line-break'> </span>"or formerly of Eliz. Rogers and easterly by land<span class='line-break'> </span>"now or late of Barber. For a more particular description<span class='line-break'> </span>"of said estate, reference may be had to my deed to<span class='line-break'> </span>"Joseph Ballister &amp; al. dated April 10, 1830, recorded<span class='line-break'> </span>"with the Suffolk Deeds, Lib. 345 fol 133.<span class='line-break'> </span>"To have and to hold the above described Estate to<span class='line-break'> </span>"said Trustees of the Newton Theological Institution<span class='line-break'> </span>"their successors and assigns, forever, upon the trusts<span class='line-break'> </span>"and for the uses hereinafter declared, viz, the said<span class='line-break'> </span>"Corporation is to pay to the Boston Fatherless and<span class='line-break'> </span>"Widows Society one half of the nett [sic] income of<span class='line-break'> </span>"said estate and of the proceeds thereof (in case the same<span class='line-break'> </span>"shall be sold) after deducting all necessary charges<span class='line-break'> </span>"of repairs, taxes and insurance and of keeping my<span class='line-break'> </span>"Tomb in Mount Auburn Cemetery in repair, such<span class='line-break'> </span>"nett income is to be applied by each of said Corporations<span class='line-break'> </span>"forever, for the promotion of the objects for which they<span class='line-break'> </span>"were severally established. And if said estate shall<span class='line-break'> </span>"be sold the income of the nett [sic] proceeds of sale be di<span class='line-break'></span>"vided equally between said two Corporations, and the<span class='line-break'> </span>"share of each be forever called the "Fennelly Fund."<span class='line-break'> </span>"No part of the principal of said funds shall be used<span class='line-break'> </span>"or expended, but the income only, forever."</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>A.J. Coolidge Esq</th> <th>I am, very respectfully,<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Secretary,</td> <td>your obt. servant,</td> </tr> <tr><td>33 School street, Boston</td> <td>John T. Heard.</td> </tr> <tr><td>Adjourned, Attest A.J. Coolidge Sec.y</td> <td>Adm'r, with the will annexed of</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>Mrs.  E.F. Gurney, deceased.</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134080">
<h3><a name="page-1134080">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 034)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>34</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees Jan. 1, 1866. '> Trustees Jan. 1, 1866. </span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn was held on Monday<span class='line-break'> </span>January 1, 1866, at 11 o'clock, a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President, and<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs Cheever, Little, Norcross and Rand,</p>
<p>Voted to dispense witht he reading of the<span class='line-break'> </span>record. -</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Perpetual Repair of Lot 1502 _ '> Perpetual Repair of Lot 1502 _ </span></p>
<p>Mr Norcross for the Committee on Lots reported<span class='line-break'> </span>that the Committee had contracted, subject to the<span class='line-break'> </span>approval of this Board, for the perpetual<span class='line-break'> </span>repair of lot numbered fifteen hundred and two<span class='line-break'> </span>(1502) belonging to the estate of the late James O. Ward.</p>
<p>Voted that said contract be concurred in.</p>
<p>Voted to adjourn to the next Monday Jan.y 8<sup>th</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>at 11 o'clock.</p>
<p>Attest Austin J. Coolidge ,, Secretary.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134082">
<h3><a name="page-1134082">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 035)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>35</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ Adjd Meeting Jan.y 8, 1866 '> Trustees _ Adj<sup>d</sup> Meeting Jan.y 8, 1866 </span></p>
<p>An adjourned meeting of the Trustees was held<span class='line-break'> </span>on Monday, January 8<sup>th</sup> at 11 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President, Messrs Adams,<span class='line-break'> </span>Austin, Bowditch, Cheever, Lovejoy, Norcross,<span class='line-break'> </span>Rand and Read. _</p>
<p>The records of the last two meetings were read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lot 3487 to be reconvd and two deeds of same to issue _ '> Lot 3487 to be reconv<sup>d</sup> and two deeds of same to issue _ </span></p>
<p>Mr Bowditch to whom was referred the petition<span class='line-break'> </span>of James C. Merrill reported, recommending<span class='line-break'> </span>that said Merrill be allowed to reconvey lot<span class='line-break'> </span>numbered 3487 to the Corporation, and that two<span class='line-break'> </span>new deeds of the same land be issued to<span class='line-break'> </span>said Merrill and Henry V. Ward. _</p>
<p>Voted to accept the report, and adopt<span class='line-break'> </span>its recommendation.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Committee chosen to defend suits vs. the Corpn on to settle by refce '> Committee chosen to defend suits vs. the Corp<sup>n</sup> on to settle by ref<sup>ce</sup> </span></p>
<p>A suit having been brought in the Superior Court for<span class='line-break'> </span>Suffolk County by the Granite Railway Company and W<sup>m</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>O'Donnell against Dr Bigelow and Messrs Read and<span class='line-break'> </span>Cheever of the Board of Trustees to recover the contract<span class='line-break'> </span>price of the facade for catacombs erected on Rosebay<span class='line-break'> </span>Avenue, it was on motion of Mr Bowditch,</p>
<p>Voted that the same Committee as were, by vote<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees, May 2, 1864, entrusted with full power to remove<span class='line-break'> </span>said facade, and make such settlement with the con<span class='line-break'></span>tractors as in their Judgment should seem just _ (viz.<span class='line-break'> </span>the President and Messrs Rand and Norcross.)<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134084">
<h3><a name="page-1134084">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 036)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>36</p>
<p>have authority to defend in the suits brought against<span class='line-break'> </span>said trustees by the Granite Railway Company and<span class='line-break'> </span>W<sup>m</sup> O'Donnell, or to settle the same by reference<span class='line-break'> </span>as in their Judgment may be deemed expedient. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Comee on Mont to Soldiers reported _ subject refd to next Board of Trustees '> Com<sup>ee</sup> on Mon<sup>t</sup> to Soldiers reported _ subject ref<sup>d</sup> to next Board of Trustees </span></p>
<p>The Committee to whom were referred the subject<span class='line-break'> </span>of a design for a monument to heroes fallen in the war,<span class='line-break'> </span>reported that they had no further plans to submit,</p>
<p>On motion of Mr Cheever,</p>
<p>Voted that the subject of the erection of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Soldiers' monument be referred to the next Board<span class='line-break'> </span>of Trustees.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Treasr asks increase of Pay. '> Treas<sup>r</sup> asks increase of Pay. </span></p>
<p>The Treasurer, Mr Bond, stated that his labors<span class='line-break'> </span>had been increased considerably by the increase of<span class='line-break'> </span>business of the Corporation, and asked instead of the<span class='line-break'> </span>present made of compensation for the last year he<span class='line-break'> </span>might be allowed to charge two and one half percent<span class='line-break'> </span>on the sales of land. _</p>
<p>Voted that the subject be referred to the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Finance, and that they be requested<span class='line-break'> </span>to report thereon at the next meeting of the Board.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Rep. for lot 3317 _'> Rep. for lot 3317 _</span></p>
<p>Upon the petition of the heirs at law of Eli Sanderson,<span class='line-break'> </span>late proprietor of lot numbered 3317, Mrs Marinda Sanderson of<span class='line-break'> </span>Brighton, his widow was designated to represent said lot. _</p>
<p>Voted that when their meeting adjourns, it be to the last Monday in<span class='line-break'> </span>January, at 11 o'clock A.M. _ Adjourned, Attest, Austin J. Coolidge<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134086">
<h3><a name="page-1134086">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 037)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>37</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Adj^d Meeting of Trustees. Jan.y. 29. 1866'>Adj^d Meeting of Trustees. Jan.y. 29. 1866</span></p>
<p>An adjourned meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>on Monday, January 29, at 11 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President and Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span>Adams, Austin, Bowditch, Cheever, Little <span class='line-break'> </span>Lovejoy, Rand, Read and Sleeper</p>
<p>The reading of the records was dispensed with.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees Annual Report'>Trustees Annual Report</span></p>
<p>The President read the Annual Report of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees, which was accepted and ordered to be printed<span class='line-break'> </span>for the Annual Meeting of the Proprietors.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Increase of Compensation of Treasurer for 1865 recommended'>Increase of Compensation of Treasurer for 1865 recommended</span></p>
<p>The Committee on Finance submitted a Report <span class='line-break'> </span>of which the following is a copy: _</p>
<p>"The Finance Committee have considered the sub<span class='line-break'></span>ject of Mr Bond's application for aditional com<span class='line-break'></span>pensation as Treasurer for the last year, and in con<span class='line-break'></span>sequence of the large increase of business of the Corporation <span class='line-break'> </span>they recommend that he be authorized to charge <span class='line-break'> </span>two and one half per cent on the sale of <span class='line-break'> </span>land for this year; _ provided, that his whole <span class='line-break'> </span>compensation, including the "Repair Fund" shall not <span class='line-break'> </span>exceed twelve hundred dollars for the year.</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>(signed)</th> <th>Charles C. Little</th> <th>}<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>Jacob Sleeper</td> <td>} Com.''</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>The Report was accepted and adopted. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134088">
<h3><a name="page-1134088">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 038)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>38</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees. Jan.y 29. 1866'>Trustees. Jan.y 29. 1866</span></p>
<p>The Annual Report of the Treasurer was then <span class='line-break'> </span>read by him.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Reports of Treasurer &amp; Superntendent'>Reports of Treasurer &amp; Superntendent</span></p>
<p>And the Annual Report of the Superintendent <span class='line-break'> </span>was read by the Secretary:</p>
<p>And they were severally accepted and ordered <span class='line-break'> </span>to be printed for the Annual Meeting of the Proprietors.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Communication of Cath. K. Baldwin respecting Tomb referred to Com. on Lots _'>Communication of Cath. K. Baldwin respecting Tomb referred to Com. on Lots _</span></p>
<p>A communication from Ctherine K. Baldwin, pro<span class='line-break'></span>prietor of lot No. 3496 making objections to the tomb built <span class='line-break'> </span>for her under the direction of the Superintendent, and <span class='line-break'> </span>one from the Superintendent explaining the business <span class='line-break'> </span>was laid before the Board: _</p>
<p>And it was Voted,</p>
<p>That the subject be referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee on Lots with full power.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Stone Steps to Anemone Path to be paid for by Corporation'>Stone Steps to Anemone Path to be paid for by Corporation</span></p>
<p>A bill of $440.00 due to Churchill, Williams &amp; Co.<span class='line-break'> </span>for furnishing granite steps at the westerly end of <span class='line-break'> </span>Anemone Path, where it rises from Spruce Avenue,<span class='line-break'> </span>ordered by Mr James Read, was laid before the Board.</p>
<p>The Board considering the steps a necessary improve<span class='line-break'></span>ment to the whole path, there being no other good entrance,<span class='line-break'> </span>it was Voted,</p>
<p>That the Treasurer be instructed to pay to <span class='line-break'> </span>Churchill, Williams &amp; Co. the sum of four hundred and <span class='line-break'> </span>forty dollars ($440.00) for a set of Granite Steps at <span class='line-break'> </span>the westerly entrance of Anemone Path out of the funds<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Corporation.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134102">
<h3><a name="page-1134102">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 045)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>45</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Lot 1597. Trustees decline to designate representative _'> Lot 1597. Trustees decline to designate representative _</span></p>
<p>In the matter of the lot of Eliza Stone late<span class='line-break'> </span>of Cambridge, deceased _ no 1597, it appearing that<span class='line-break'> </span>she died unmarried, leaving a father Isaac Stone,<span class='line-break'> </span>who would be the inheritor of anything not devised<span class='line-break'> </span>in the will to any other person, and by the terms<span class='line-break'> </span>of her will it appearing that said lot had descen<span class='line-break'></span>ded to her said father, it was</p>
<p>Voted that the Trustees decline to make any<span class='line-break'> </span>designation of representative for this lot. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Com. on Lots. on Lots Kept in repair _'> Report of Com. on Lots. on Lots Kept in repair _</span></p>
<p>Mr Austin for the Committee on Lots<span class='line-break'> </span>submitted the Annual Report of the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on the visitation of lots kept in repair under the<span class='line-break'> </span>Repair Fund. _</p>
<p>Voted that the report be accepted and<span class='line-break'> </span>placed on file. _</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Adjourned sine die.</th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>Attest Austin J. Coolidge</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Secretary.</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>
</div>

<div id="page-1134104">
<h3><a name="page-1134104">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 046)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>46</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Proprietors Annual Meeting _ Feb.y 5. 1866. '> Proprietors Annual Meeting _ Feb.y 5. 1866. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn Cemetery.</p>
<p>The Annual Meeting of the Proprietors of the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn will be held at the Horticultural<span class='line-break'> </span>Hall, corner of Fremont and Bromfield streets, Boston, on<span class='line-break'> </span>Monday February 5<sup>th</sup> at 3½ o'clock p.m., to hear<span class='line-break'> </span>the annual reports and choose Trustees for the ensuing<span class='line-break'> </span>year. _</p>
<p>Jany. 29, 1866. Austin J. Coolidge, Secretary.</p>
<p>In accordance with the foregoing notification which was<span class='line-break'> </span>published seven days before the time of meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>in several Boston newspapers, the Proprietors<span class='line-break'> </span>met at the time and place therein named.</p>
<p>A quorum being in attendance, Dr. Jacob<span class='line-break'> </span>Bigelow took the Chair.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Records _ '> Records _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The record of the last Annual Meeting was<span class='line-break'> </span>read by the Secretary.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Acceptance, &amp;c of Annual Report _ '> Acceptance, &amp;c of Annual Report _ </span></p>
<p>The President has proceeded to read a portion of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Annual Report of the Trustees, when</p>
<p>On motion of Rufus Wyman Esq. the meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>voted to dispense with the reading of the several reports,<span class='line-break'> </span>the same having been distributed in printed form to<span class='line-break'> </span>the proprietors present. _</p>
<p>On motion of Nathan Matthews Esq</p>
<p>Voted to accept the Reports, &amp; that they be placed on file.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134106">
<h3><a name="page-1134106">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 047)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>47</p>
<p>Some informal discussion ensued in relation to the<span class='line-break'> </span>different ballots placed in the hands of the members<span class='line-break'> </span>present, when</p>
<p>On motion of Charles Thompson Esq.</p>
<p>Voted that the meeting proceed to ballot for<span class='line-break'> </span>trustees for the ensuing year. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Committee to Receive and Count Votes for Trustees _'> Committee to Receive and Count Votes for Trustees _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of W<sup>m</sup> B. Towne Esq.</p>
<p>Voted that a Committee of five be appointed to<span class='line-break'> </span>receive, assort and count the votes for Trustees.</p>
<p>The chairman appointed<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>{ Sidney Homer<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>{ Benj. F. White</td> </tr> <tr><td>Messrs</td> <td>{ Ichabod Howland</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>{ Chas. Hamilton Parker</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>{ Chas. U. Cotting</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Order upon mode of ballotting '> Order upon mode of ballotting </span></p>
<p>On motion of Jeffrey Richardson Esq.</p>
<p>Voted</p>
<p>That no single ballot and no collection<span class='line-break'> </span>of proxy ballots shall be received and<span class='line-break'> </span>counted unless marked with the name of<span class='line-break'> </span>the depositor. _</p>
<p>After some delay in counting the votes.<span class='line-break'> </span>The Committee submitted their report in<span class='line-break'> </span>the words following: _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<h3><a name="page-1134112">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 051)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>51</p>
<p>This certifies that we have examined the books<span class='line-break'> </span>and accounts of the Treasurer of the Treasurer of the Propri<span class='line-break'></span>etors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn for the year ending <span class='line-break'> </span>December 30. 1865, and have found them correctly kept and <span class='line-break'> </span>properly balanced, with satisfactory vouchers for all payments <span class='line-break'> </span>charged.</p>
<p>The Certificates of Stocks and other evidences of property were<span class='line-break'> </span>found in accordance with the statements in his accounts.</p>
<p>In the fund for Repairs there appears to be a balance <span class='line-break'> </span>of $1.417.42, and in the General Account $7.917.39.</p>

<div id="page-1134113">
<h3><a name="page-1134113">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 052)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>52</p>
<p>Permanent Fund.</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134114">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 053)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>53</p>
<p>Trustees' Records _ 1866-7.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees- Feb.y. 1866 _ meeting for Organization _'>Trustees- Feb.y. 1866 _ meeting for Organization _</span></p>
<p>The first meeting of the Trustees for organi<span class='line-break'></span>zation and business was held at the office of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation (33 School Street,) on Monday February <span class='line-break'> </span>19<sup>th</sup> 1866, at 11 O'clock a.m. _</p>
<p>There were present Messrs Adams, Austin, <span class='line-break'> </span>Bigelow, Bowditch, Cheever, Livermore, Lovejoy, <span class='line-break'> </span>Norcross, Rand and Read. _ 10</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting of the Trustees <span class='line-break'> </span>and of the Annual Meeting of the Proprietors was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Ballot for Officers and Committees '>Ballot for Officers and Committees </span></p>
<p>The Board then proceeded to the choice<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Officers and Committees by ballot, and <span class='line-break'> </span>they were declared to be unanimously chosen as <span class='line-break'> </span>follows: _</p>
<p><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>President -</th> <th>Dr. Jacob Bigelow<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Secretary --</td> <td>Austin J. Coolidge</td> </tr> <tr><td>Treasurer-</td> <td>George W<sup>m</sup> Bond</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>___</th> <th>{ Little<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Finance</td> <td>Messrs</td> <td>{ Sleeper</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>___</th> <th>{ Austin<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Com<sup>ee</sup> on Lots</td> <td>Messrs</td> <td>{ Norcross</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>{ Bowditch</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>

<div id="page-1134116">
<h3><a name="page-1134116">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 055)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>55</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee on Iron Fence _'>Committee on Iron Fence _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the same Committee that was chosen <span class='line-break'> </span>on the 4<sup>th</sup> of December last, to consider the Expediency of <span class='line-break'> </span>enclosing the Stone Farm with an Iron fence on the <span class='line-break'> </span>road, to make inquiries obtain estimates and report <span class='line-break'> </span>at a future meeting - viz.  <span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>{ Cheever<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Messrs</td> <td>{ Bowditch</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>{ &amp; Lovejoy </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> be rechosen with the same powers. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Railway tickets to be purchased for Trustees _'>Railway tickets to be purchased for Trustees _</span></p>
<p>Voted that the Secretary be authorized to pur<span class='line-break'></span>chase for the use of this Board one hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>and twenty car tickets of the Union Railway Company<span class='line-break'> </span>from Boston to Mount Auburn, and distribute <span class='line-break'> </span>them to the Trustees.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Perpetual Repair _ Lot 2517.'>Perpetual Repair _ Lot 2517.</span></p>
<p>The Secretary reported that the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>on Lots had contracted for the perpetual re<span class='line-break'></span>pair of Lot No 2517 belonging to the estate of <span class='line-break'> </span>the late Josiah Vose for the sum of Eleven <span class='line-break'> </span>hundred dollars ($1100) subject to the concurrence <span class='line-break'> </span>of this Board.</p>
<p>Voted that said contract be concurred in.</p>
<p>Voted that when this meeting adjourn,<span class='line-break'> </span>it be to the next regular meeting on the 1<sup>st</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>Monday in March. _</p>
<p>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>Attest Austin J. Coolidge Secretary,</p>
<p>[Note: the following written vertically in the left hand margin at the bottom of the page:]</p>
<p>Commonwealth of Massachusetts</p>
<p>Norfolk ss Feby 19. 1866.  There personally ap<span class='line-break'></span>peared Austin J. Coolidge and made oath that <span class='line-break'> </span>he would faithfully perform the duties of Secretary of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn.</p>
<p>Before me</p>
<p><u>Bradford Kingman</u> ,, Justice of the Peace.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134117">
<h3><a name="page-1134117">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 056)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>56</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees - March 5. 1866.'>Trustees - March 5. 1866.</span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trus<span class='line-break'></span>tees was held on Monday, March 5<sup>th</sup>.<span class='line-break'> </span>1866, at 11 O'clock a.m. –</p>
<p>There were present the President, and <span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs Adams, Austin, Cheever, Little, Liver<span class='line-break'></span>more, Lovejoy and Rand. _ 8</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Declaration respecting ownership of two or more ten-ants in common of one lot not to be recorded.'>Declaration respecting ownership of two or more ten-ants in common of one lot not to be recorded.</span></p>
<p>The Secretary presented the request of H. N. &amp; M. J. <span class='line-break'> </span>Doyle that an instrument purporting to be a<span class='line-break'> </span>declaration in trust in respect to lot No. 940,<span class='line-break'> </span>might be recorded on the books of this Corporation.</p>
<p>Voted that the Secretary be instructed to <span class='line-break'> </span>inform the Messrs Doyle that the said instrument <span class='line-break'> </span>cannot be recorded with the records of this <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Iron Fence to be painted. '>Iron Fence to be painted. </span></p>
<p>Voted that the Committee on Grounds be authorized <span class='line-break'> </span>to cause the Iron Fence enclosing the Cemetery <span class='line-break'> </span>to be painted, at an expense not exceeding nine <span class='line-break'> </span>hundred dollars. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Committee on Salaries _'>Report of Committee on Salaries _</span></p>
<p>Mr Rand for the Special Committee appointed <span class='line-break'> </span>at the last meeting to consider what salaries <span class='line-break'> </span>shall be paid the several officers, submitted their <span class='line-break'> </span>report: and upon motion by him, it was</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Referred to [next Meeting _]'>Referred to [next Meeting _]</span></p>
<p>Voted that the consideration of the report</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134118">
<h3><a name="page-1134118">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 057)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>57</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' [Referred to] next Meeting _ '> [Referred to] next Meeting _ </span></p>
<p>be referred to the next meeting.</p>
<p>An order which was recommended by the<span class='line-break'> </span>report was then proposed by Mr Rand,<span class='line-break'> </span>which after amendment, was adopted,<span class='line-break'> </span>and is as follows: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Treasr, Sec.y, Supt or Gatekeeper not to sell lots on commisn _'> Treas<sup>r</sup>, Sec.y, Sup<sup>t</sup> or Gatekeeper not to sell lots on commis<sup>n</sup> _</span></p>
<p>"Resolved that the Treasurer, Secretary,<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent and Gatekeeper be and they are<span class='line-break'> </span>hereby directed in no case to act as paid<span class='line-break'> </span>agents or brokers for the sale or exchange of<span class='line-break'> </span>lots, and are hereby forbidden to receive any<span class='line-break'> </span>commission, fee or reward for negotiating or<span class='line-break'> </span>effecting such sales or exchanges." _</p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned.</p>
<p>Attest Austin J. Coolidge Sec.y</p>
<p>---------------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees - April 2, 1866 - '> Trustees - April 2, 1866 - </span></p>
<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held on Monday, April 2, 1866, at<span class='line-break'> </span>11 o'clock a.m. _</p>
<p>There were present the President, and<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs. Cheever, Norcross, Rand and Read. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p>The report of the Committee on Salaries was taken<span class='line-break'> </span>from the table and read. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134119">
<h3><a name="page-1134119">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 058)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>58</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees - April 2. 1866 '> Trustees - April 2. 1866 </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Com. on Salaries taken from table _'> Report of Com. on Salaries taken from table _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was agreed to take up the subject, acting upon<span class='line-break'> </span>the question relating to the salary of each offices _ sep<span class='line-break'></span>arately.</p>
<p>It was moved by Mr Rand,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='The vote for adoption being insufficient, it was postponed _'>The vote for adoption being insufficient, it was postponed _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>That the salary of the Superintendent be the amount<span class='line-break'> </span>recommended by the Committee viz. 2250. _</p>
<p>The question being taken, and then not appearing<span class='line-break'> </span>to be five votes for its adoption,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Vote for postponet reconsidered _ and Report recommitted to same Comee '> Vote for postpone<sup>t</sup> reconsidered _ and Report recommitted to same Com<sup>ee</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr Rand,</p>
<p>Voted that the whole question of salaries be<span class='line-break'> </span>over until the next meeting.</p>
<p>Subsequently, on motion by Mr Norcross, it was</p>
<p>Voted that the vote whereby the report of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Salaries be postponed to the next meeting<span class='line-break'> </span>be reconsidred: _</p>
<p>It was then</p>
<p>Voted to recommit the report to<span class='line-break'> </span>the same Committee with all accompanying papers.</p>
<p>--------------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Time of meeting of the Trustees _'> Time of meeting of the Trustees _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr Read,</p>
<p>Voted that hereafter the meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>be held at 10 o'clock instead of 11 o'clock _</p>

Hadley, tenants in common of lot numbered 3591.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Attest Austin J. <p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Conveyance _ Corporation to Mary Hemenway and Mary Hemenway to Corporation _ Dated May 5, 1866 _'> Conveyance _ Corporation to Mary Hemenway and Mary Hemenway to Corporation _ Dated May 5, 1866 _</span></p>
<p>Conveyance to and Release from</p>
<p>Mary Hemenway</p>
<p>[ left arrow ] ––––––––––– [ right arrow ]</p>
<p>Whereas the Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn have by their deed heretofore, to wit, on the Eleventh<span class='line-break'> </span>day of December, A.D. Eighteen hundreed and sixty three,<span class='line-break'> </span>conveyed to Mary Hemenway of Boston, in the county<span class='line-break'> </span>of Suffolk and Commonwealth of Massachusetts certain<span class='line-break'> </span>land in said Cemetery for onramental purposes, bounded<span class='line-break'> </span>on the southerly side by Cowslip Path, and on the northerly<span class='line-break'> </span>side by Thistle Path, as said paths were then laid down,<span class='line-break'> </span>on a plan accompanying said deed, containing fif<span class='line-break'></span>teen thousand two hundred and five square feet, more<span class='line-break'> </span>or less, which deed and plan are recorded with the records<span class='line-break'> </span>of the doings of the Trustees and the Corporation in volume<span class='line-break'> </span>3<sup>d</sup> huge 309, said land being occupied in part by a<span class='line-break'> </span>basin and fountain;</p>
<p>And whereas, for the mutual con<span class='line-break'></span>venience of both parties to said deed a change of the Crea<span class='line-break'></span>tion of said Cowslip Path has been proposed, whereby<span class='line-break'> </span>said path will be brought nearer to said fountain, and<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134125">
<h3><a name="page-1134125">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 064)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>64</p>
<p>cut off a wedge from the land heretofore conveyed,<span class='line-break'> </span>to the said Mary Hemenway, and the said Mary<span class='line-break'> </span>Hemenway is desirous to take are equivalent<span class='line-break'> </span>amount of land upon the westerly side of said<span class='line-break'> </span>fountain in Exchange therefor.</p>
<p>Now this Indenture<span class='line-break'> </span>witnesseth that the said Proprietors of the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn, in consideration of the premises,<span class='line-break'> </span>and of the release hereinafter made on the part of<span class='line-break'> </span>the said Mary Hemenway, hereby grant, bargain,<span class='line-break'> </span>sell and convey to the said Mary Hemenway, her<span class='line-break'> </span>heirs and assigns forever, the two parcels of land<span class='line-break'> </span>marked A and B upon the plan hereto annexed,<span class='line-break'> </span>(a duplicate copy of said plan being entered with the<span class='line-break'> </span>records of said Corporation,) situated upon the westerly<span class='line-break'> </span>side of said fountain between Cistus Path and<span class='line-break'> </span>Spruce Avenue and containing nine hundred and thirty<span class='line-break'> </span>five and 47/100 feet, more or less.</p>
<p>To have a to hold the same to the said<span class='line-break'> </span>Mary Hemenway, her heirs and assigns to her and their<span class='line-break'> </span>own use forever, but only for ornamental purposes,<span class='line-break'> </span>and subject to the same conditions and restrictions<span class='line-break'> </span>as are contained in the aforementioned deed.</p>
<p>And the said Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn do hereby covenant to and with the said Mary<span class='line-break'> </span>Hemenway her heirs and assigns that they are<span class='line-break'> </span>lawfully seized of the aforegranted premises and of </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134126">
<h3><a name="page-1134126">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 064a)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>[This page is inserted between page 64 and 65 containing a map of the areajust deeded to Mary Hemenway for ornamental use in general and Alice Fountain in particular.]</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134127">
<h3><a name="page-1134127">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 065)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>65</p>
<p>the ways leading to the same from the highway, in fee<span class='line-break'> </span>simple; that they are free from all incumbran<span class='line-break'></span>ces; that the Corporation have a right to sell and<span class='line-break'> </span>convey the said premises to the said Mary Hem<span class='line-break'></span>enway for the purposes above expressed; and that<span class='line-break'> </span>they will warrant and defend the same to the said<span class='line-break'> </span>Mary Hemenway her heirs and assigns forever.</p>
<p>And the said Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn for the covenant to and with the said Mary<span class='line-break'> </span>Hemenway her heirs and assigns, that the provisions<span class='line-break'> </span>of an order passed by the Trustees of this Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span>on the 6<sup>th</sup> day of April 1857, for the establishment and<span class='line-break'> </span>security of a fund for the preservation of the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>and its appurtenances, and the further provisions<span class='line-break'> </span>of an order adopted by said Trustees on the 4<sup>th</sup> day<span class='line-break'> </span>of November A.D. 1861, requiring that certain spaces<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Cemetery be forever kept open, and that no inter<span class='line-break'></span>ments be ever made, nor buildings nor monuments<span class='line-break'> </span>of any description be erected thereon (both which are<span class='line-break'> </span>made parts of this covenant as if herein repeated,)<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be forever kept, observed and performed by said<span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation.</p>
<p>And the said Mary Hemenway in con<span class='line-break'></span>sideration of the premises, and of the conveyance of said<span class='line-break'> </span>land last herein described, doth hereby forever remise,<span class='line-break'> </span>release, and quitclaim to said Proprietors of the Cem<span class='line-break'></span>etery of Mount Auburn, all the land situated upon<span class='line-break'> </span>the southerly side of the northerly line of Cowslip</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1134128">
<h3><a name="page-1134128">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 066)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>66</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' (See p. 311, vol III for original contract.) '> (See p. 311, vol III for original contract.) </span></p>
<p>Path, as shown upon the above named plan, -<span class='line-break'> </span>a duplicate copy of which is to be entered with<span class='line-break'> </span>the record of this conveyance upon the records of said<span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation - said land so released containing<span class='line-break'> </span>nine hundred and thirty five and 47/100 square feet,<span class='line-break'> </span>more or less.</p>
<p>To have and to hold the same to the<span class='line-break'> </span>Proprietors of the Cemetery of Mount Auburn, their suc<span class='line-break'></span>cessors and assigns forever.</p>
<p>And the said Mary<span class='line-break'> </span>Hemenway for herself and her heirs, Executors and admin<span class='line-break'></span>istrators doth covenant with the said Proprietors of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn their successors and assigns that the<span class='line-break'> </span>premises are free from all incumbrances made or suffered by her;<span class='line-break'> </span>and that the will, and her heirs, Executors and administrators<span class='line-break'> </span>shall warrant and defend the same to be said Proprietors their suc<span class='line-break'></span>cessors and assigns forever against the lawful claims and demands<span class='line-break'> </span>of all persons claiming by through or under her, but against<span class='line-break'> </span>none other.</p>

<p>In witness whereof the said Corporation hath caused these pres<span class='line-break'></span>ents to be signed by the Treasurer and countersigned by the Secretary,<span class='line-break'> </span>and the Corporate seal to be hereto affixed; and the said<span class='line-break'> </span>Mary Hemenway hath also signed her name and affixed<span class='line-break'> </span>her seal on this fifth day of May A.D.<span class='line-break'> </span>Eighteen hundred and sixty six.</p>
