<div id="page-1134215">
<h3><a name="page-1134215">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 153)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>153</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='as Represen-tative of Lot 236 rejected _'>as Represen-tative of Lot 236 rejected _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Reported in writing _</p>
<p>That the charter authorizes the Trustees to designate <span class='line-break'> </span>the representative of a lot only from the "devisers or heirs <span class='line-break'> </span>at law" of a deceased proprietor: _ that the Rev<sup>d</sup> Dr <span class='line-break'> </span>Miles is not either a devisee or heir at law, although <span class='line-break'> </span>a part owner, and therefore not eligible to said appointment.</p>
<p>He therefore recommended that the petition be not granted.</p>
<p>The report was accepted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Perpetual Repair of Lot 3281 _'>Perpetual Repair of Lot 3281 _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary reported that the Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>on Lots had contracted with Edwin Booth, <span class='line-break'> </span>the proprietor of lot numbered thirty two hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>and eighty one (3281) for the perpetual care of said <span class='line-break'> </span>lot on payment of five hundred and fifty dollars.</p>
<p>Voted that said contract be ratified.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Story Lot Fund _ Story Statue Fund _'>Story Lot Fund _ Story Statue Fund _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Treasurer suggested the adoption of the fol<span class='line-break'></span>lowing vote, which was passed: _</p>
<p>"That the Committee on Lots be instructed to <span class='line-break'> </span>direct the Treasurer how to charge the bills paid in <span class='line-break'> </span>1864 for improvements to the lot of the late Joseph <span class='line-break'> </span>Story; and to ascertain if, in any way, the balance <span class='line-break'> </span>of the fund for the Story Statue can be appro<span class='line-break'></span>priated thereto."<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th><small>Adjourned to the next regular meeting. </small><span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td><small>Attest, Austin J. Coolidge </small></td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td><small>Secretary. </small></td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>

<h3><a name="page-1134216">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 154)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>154</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees March 10, 1868'>Trustees March 10, 1868</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular meeting of the Trustees (the same <span class='line-break'> </span>being an adjournment of the meeting for organization) <span class='line-break'> </span>was held at the rooms, 16 Pemberton Square, on <span class='line-break'> </span>Tuesday, March 10<sup>th</sup> 1868, at 10 o'clock a.m. _</p>
<p>There were present Messrs Adams, Bowditch, <span class='line-break'> </span>Cheever, Little, Livermore, Lovejoy, and Sleeper. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Chairman pro tempore'>Chairman pro tempore</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President not having arrived, Mr Little <span class='line-break'> </span>was chosen Chariman pro tem. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p>The President and Mr Read here came in. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of Committee on Salary of Secretary _ viz. $1350 _ and room rent free _'>Report of Committee on Salary of Secretary _ viz. $1350 _ and room rent free _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Livermore of the Committee to which was referred <span class='line-break'> </span>the communication of the Secretary with regard to an <span class='line-break'> </span>increase of his salary, and relative to an assistant <span class='line-break'> </span>in his office, reported: _</p>
<p>"That they recommend that the <span class='line-break'> </span>salary continue to be the same as last year, viz. $1350, <span class='line-break'> </span>and that the Secretary have the use of the small room <span class='line-break'> </span>leased by this Company free of rent, for the purpose of <span class='line-break'> </span>transacting his private business _ the large room to be <span class='line-break'> </span>kept for the sole use of this Company, which is to pay all <span class='line-break'> </span>the expenses of both rooms as specified in their lease." _</p>
<p>The Committee do not recommend any action <span class='line-break'> </span>in relation to an Assistant."<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Isaac Livermore</th> <th>}<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Signed</td> <td>James Cheever</td> <td>} Com<sup>ee</sup></td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>James Read</td> <td>}</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134217">
<h3><a name="page-1134217">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 155)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>155</p>
<p>Voted that the report of this committee be <span class='line-break'> </span>accepted and adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report on Story Lot Fund _ &amp; Story Statue Fund _'>Report on Story Lot Fund _ &amp; Story Statue Fund _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Bowditch for the Committee on Lots pre<span class='line-break'></span>sented the report of the Committee upon the subject of <span class='line-break'> </span>the vote adopted at the February meeting relating to <span class='line-break'> </span>the fund for the care of the Story Lot, and the balance <span class='line-break'> </span>of the fund in the hands of the Treasurer for the Story <span class='line-break'> </span>Statue. _</p>
<p>The report was accepted, and the following <span class='line-break'> </span>vote was adopted: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Rept on Story Statue Fund recommitted _'>Rep<sup>t</sup> on Story Statue Fund recommitted _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>"That so much of the subject of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Committee's Report as relates to the balance of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Story fund be recommitted, with authority to obtain <span class='line-break'> </span>the consent of the living subscribers of that fund for <span class='line-break'> </span>the disposition of said balance." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Resolutions in favor of duties of Sec.y &amp; Treasr being done at one office _'>Resolutions in favor of duties of Sec.y &amp; Treas<sup>r</sup> being done at one office _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Bowditch presented the following resolutions <span class='line-break'> </span>which were unanimously adopted: _</p>
<p>"That it is the opinion of this Board that the <span class='line-break'> </span>convenience of the Corporation and the Proprietors of lots <span class='line-break'> </span>in the Cemetery requires that the duties of the Secretary <span class='line-break'> </span>and Treasurer should be performed at the same office, <span class='line-break'> </span>and that the rooms hired by the Trustees on lease furnish <span class='line-break'> </span>the most desirable location."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee to confer with Treasr _'>Com<sup>ee</sup> to confer with Treas<sup>r</sup> _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>"That a Committee be chosen to confer with<span class='line-break'> </span>the Treasurer, and report to the Trustees upon the subject<span class='line-break'> </span>of the foregoing resolution."</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134218">
<h3><a name="page-1134218">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 156)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>156</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees March 10, 1868'>Trustees March 10, 1868</span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was further noted _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Committee to confer with Treasr _'>Committee to confer with Treas<sup>r</sup> _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>That said Committee <span class='line-break'> </span>consist of three: and upon nomination by <span class='line-break'> </span>the President<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Messrs</th> <th>Austin<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Read and</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Norcross</td> <td>were so chosen. _</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='New Boiler for Engine recommended by Sup t _ referred to Com. on Grounds.'>New Boiler for Engine recommended by Sup <sup>t</sup> _ referred to Com. on Grounds.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>A communication from the Superintendent was read, <span class='line-break'> </span>recommending, upon the opinion of experts, an exchange <span class='line-break'> </span>of the old boiler of the engine at the Cemetery for a <span class='line-break'> </span>new one, and stating the probable cost of such ex<span class='line-break'></span>change to be within one thousand dollars,</p>
<p>upon which it was</p>
<p>Voted that the subject of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent's communication be referred to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Grounds with full power: and <span class='line-break'> </span>that a sum not exceeding one thousand dollars <span class='line-break'> </span>be appropriated therefor, if the Committee shall deem <span class='line-break'> </span>the work necessary. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Perpetual Repair of Lot 2144 _'>Perpetual Repair of Lot 2144 _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary reported that the Committee on Lots <span class='line-break'> </span>had contracted with John Woods the proprietor of lot <span class='line-break'> </span>numbered twenty one hundred and forty four (2144) <span class='line-break'> </span>for the perpetual care of said lot on payment of <span class='line-break'> </span>three hundred and fifty dollars, ($350).</p>
<p>Voted that said contract be ratified. _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>

<div id="page-1134219">
<h3><a name="page-1134219">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 157)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Representation of Lots _'>Representation of Lots _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Upon the petition of the parties in interest <span class='line-break'> </span>representatives were designated for the lots in connec<span class='line-break'></span>tion with which they are named as follows: _</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees April 14, 1868'>Trustees <date when='1868-04-14'>April 14, 1868</date></span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular meeting of the Trustees was held <span class='line-break'> </span>at their rooms on Tuesday, <date when='1868-04-14'>April 14, 1868</date>, <span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock a.m. ~</p>
<p>There were present the President and Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span>Bowditch, Cheever, Livermore, Norcross, Read <span class='line-break'> </span>and Sleeper. _ 7</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Verbal Report of Comee to confer with the Treasurer _'>Verbal Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> to confer with the Treasurer _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>In the absence of the Chairman, Mr Norcross, for <span class='line-break'> </span>the Commitee chosen at the last meeting to confer <span class='line-break'> </span>with the Treasurer, stated verbally that Mr Bond <span class='line-break'> </span>agreed in view with the Trustees that the interests <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Corporation would be advanced if the duties <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Treasurer should be performed at this <span class='line-break'> </span>office, but that his business engagements would <span class='line-break'> </span>not allow him to retain the office, if transferred.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Comee authorized to consider the whole subject of Office of Treasr &amp; report _'>Com<sup>ee</sup> authorized to consider the whole subject of Office of Treas<sup>r</sup> &amp; report _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was then</p>
<p>Voted that the Committee on the office <span class='line-break'> </span>of Treasurer be authorized to consider the whole <span class='line-break'> </span>subject and report to this Board. _</p>

<p>After some debate it was</p>
<p>Voted that the matter</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='1788'>1788</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Calvin Emery Morse of Cambridge port, son of Calvin <span class='line-break'> </span>Morse, deceased prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 1788;</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='2308'>2308</span><span class='line-break'> </span>(Rev.) Stephen G. Bulfinch of Cambridge, brother of Thomas <span class='line-break'> </span>Bulfinch, deceased prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 2308. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='The Secretary authorized to appear in suit brought by H.N. Gardner.'>The Secretary authorized to appear in suit brought by H.N. Gardner.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary stated that one Henry N. Gardner, <span class='line-break'> </span>who was nearly two years since excluded from working <span class='line-break'> </span>on lots in the Cemetery, by vote of the Trustees, and <span class='line-break'> </span>who failed in an equity suit against the Corporation, had <span class='line-break'> </span>brought an action at law against the Corporation.</p>
<p>Voted that the Secretary confer with Mr Rand, and <span class='line-break'> </span>attend to the defense of the suit by the said Gardner.</p>
<p>The meeting was then adjourned to <date when='1868-04-21'>Tuesday, 21</date><sup>st</sup> at 10 o'clock.</p>
<p>Attest Austin J. Coolidge, Sec.y<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p>Mr Austin, as Chairman, submitted the fol<span class='line-break'></span>lowing report: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Comee on Office of Treasurer _ '> Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> on Office of Treasurer _ </span></p>
<p>"The Committee to whom was referred<span class='line-break'> </span>the subject of 'requiring the Treasurer and Secretary to<span class='line-break'> </span>perform their duties at the office of the Corporation'</p>
<p>Respectfully Report:</p>
<p>That they have had a conference with<span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Bond, the Treasurer, who fully agreed with the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee in opinion as to the necessity of such an arrange<span class='line-break'></span>ment, but stating however, that his engagement would<span class='line-break'> </span>prevent his holding the office of Treasurer, except under<span class='line-break'> </span>the present arrangement. _</p>
<p>Your Committee is, nevertheless, unan<span class='line-break'></span>imously of opinion, and do recommend, that the Treasurer<span class='line-break'> </span>and Secretary of this Corporation be required to attend<span class='line-break'> </span>to the duties pertaining to their office at the no. 16 Pem<span class='line-break'></span>berton Square, between the hours of nine a.m. and<span class='line-break'> </span>three p.m. of each working day, and that the Records,<span class='line-break'> </span>Books of account and other papers of the Corporation be<span class='line-break'> </span>kept at the same place, until otherwise ordered by<span class='line-break'> </span>the Trustees.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Respectfully submitted<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Edward Austin</td> <td>}</td> </tr> <tr><td><date when='1868-04-06'>April 6, 1868</date></td> <td>___</td> <td>James Read</td> <td>} Committee ''</td> </tr> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Otis Norcross</td> <td>}</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>The report was accepted, and the<span class='line-break'> </span>following vote was then adopted: _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p>Art. 6<sup>th</sup>,</p>
<p>in the 1<sup>st</sup> line, substitute <u>"ten"</u> for <u>"five"</u>: _</p>
<p>In 8<sup>th</sup> line, after the word "Expenditure" strike out six<span class='line-break'> </span>lines to word "moneys" inclusive, and insert _<span class='line-break'> </span>"and such bills for incidental Expenses as may<span class='line-break'> </span>be contracted at Mount Auburn by the Superin<span class='line-break'></span>tendent, or at the office in Boston by the Secretary, as<span class='line-break'> </span>the President may approve. He shall deposit all<span class='line-break'> </span>moneys received in such bank in Boston as the<span class='line-break'> </span>Finance Committee shall direct to the credit of the Corpor<span class='line-break'></span>ation, and all checks for moneys drawn from the bank<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be signed by the Treasurer and countersigned by<span class='line-break'> </span>one or more of the Committee of Finance, ^<sup>and in the absence of said Corp. by one or more members of the Board _</sup> He shall,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' see p 169 _'> see p 169 _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>under the direction of the Committee of Finance, invest<span class='line-break'> </span>the surplus moneys, keep proper books of account,<span class='line-break'> </span>and quarterly, at the first meetings of the Trustees in the<span class='line-break'> </span>months of January, April, July and October, be shall<span class='line-break'> </span>lay before the Board a balance sheet showing the<span class='line-break'> </span>transactions of the quarter prior to the first day of<span class='line-break'> </span>the current month; and also a statement in detail<span class='line-break'> </span>of the balances held by the Corporation for the repair of<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ May 12, 1868. '> Trustees _ <date when='1868-05-12'>May 12, 1868</date>. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular meeting of the Trustees of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery of Mount Auburn was held on<span class='line-break'> </span>Tuesday, <date when='1868-05-12'>May 12<sup>th</sup>, 1868</date>, at 10 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President, and Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span>Adams, Austin, Bowditch, Cheever, Livermore<span class='line-break'> </span>and Norcross. _ 7 _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Resignation of Mr Bond as Treasr &amp; acceptance of same _ '> Resignation of Mr Bond as Treas<sup>r</sup> &amp; acceptance of same _ </span></p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read and<span class='line-break'> </span>approved.</p>
<p>The letter of resignation of the Treasurer, Mr Bond having been read,</p>
<p>On motion by Mr Livermore,</p>
<p>Voted that Mr Bond's resignation be accepted<span class='line-break'> </span>to take effect on the first of June next. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134229">
<h3><a name="page-1134229">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 167)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>167</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report on nomination of Treasurer reconsidered, amended _ &amp; accepted _ '> Report on nomination of Treasurer reconsidered, amended _ &amp; accepted _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted to reconsider the report submitted and<span class='line-break'> </span>accepted at the last meeting on the nomination<span class='line-break'> </span>of a Treasurer _</p>
<p>Voted to amend a verbal error in the report by<span class='line-break'> </span>striking out "2500" and inserting "2350." _</p>
<p>The report as thus amended was then accepted.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Adoption of amendt to Art. VI of By-Laws _'> Adoption of amend<sup>t</sup> to Art. VI of By-Laws _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The amendments proposed at the last meeting to Article<span class='line-break'> </span>sixth of the Bylaws _ "Treasurer", were taken from<span class='line-break'> </span>the table, read and adopted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Choice of Treasurer _ '> Choice of Treasurer _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was then</p>
<p>Voted to proceed to the choice of<span class='line-break'> </span>a Treasurer, to fill the vacancy occasioned by<span class='line-break'> </span>the resignation of Mr Bond. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' A.J. Coolidge chosen _ '> A.J. Coolidge chosen _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President appointed Mr Livermore a Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee to receive and count the ballots: _<span class='line-break'> </span>and he reported that seven ballots were cast,<span class='line-break'> </span>all of which were given for</p>
<p>Austin J. Coolidge.</p>
<p>and he was declared to be duly chosen Treasurer.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Finance Comee to audit accts, of present Treasr to [deliver property to his successor upon taking bond &amp;c _]'> Finance Com<sup>ee</sup> to audit accts, of present Treas<sup>r</sup> to [deliver property to his successor upon taking bond &amp;c _]</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the Committee of Finance be re<span class='line-break'></span>quested to audit the accounts of the present Treasurer,<span class='line-break'> </span>to the <date when='1868-06-01'>1<sup>st</sup> of June next</date>, and to deliver to his successor, upon<span class='line-break'> </span>receiving a satisfactory bond, all books, papers, funds,</p>

<p>They had left in the hands of the late Treas<span class='line-break'></span>urer for a short period, certain of the books contain<span class='line-break'></span>ing the unsettled accounts, for the purpose of fa<span class='line-break'></span>cilitating a settlement of said accounts.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' July 14, 1868 _ Trustees _'> <date when='1868-07-14'>July 14, 1868</date> _ Trustees _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular meeting of the Trustees was<span class='line-break'> </span>held on Tuesday, <date when='1868-07-14'>July 14<sup>th</sup> 1868</date>, at 10 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present, the President, and<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs. Cheever, Livermore, Norcross, Rand and<span class='line-break'> </span>Sleeper. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Proposal to sell Wyeth House &amp; Land to Corporation _'> Proposal to sell Wyeth House &amp; Land to Corporation _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President read a communication from<span class='line-break'> </span>Alexander M<sup>c</sup>Donald offering to sell to this Corporation the<span class='line-break'> </span>house and land belonging to and occupied by Misses Eliz<span class='line-break'></span>abeth and Mary Wyeth, nearly opposite to Mount Auburn Gate, as<span class='line-break'> </span><small>soon as he should obtain the conveyance from them, for the sum of four</small><span class='line-break'> </span>thousand dollars ($4,000),. This offer was accompanied by the written<span class='line-break'> </span>proposal of the Misses Wyeth.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Special Comee authorized to purchase _'> Special Com<sup>ee</sup> authorized to purchase _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was thereupon</p>
<p>Voted that the President and<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs. Cheever and Livermore be a committee<span class='line-break'> </span>with full power to purchase, if they deem it<span class='line-break'> </span>expedient, the estate of the Misses Wyeth nearly<span class='line-break'> </span>opposite Mount Auburn Gate.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Appropriation to purchase Wyeth House moved _'> Appropriation to purchase Wyeth House moved _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>It was further</p>
<p>Moved that the sum of four<span class='line-break'> </span>thousand dollars ($4,000.00) be hereby appro<span class='line-break'></span>priated for the purchase of said Wyeth estate,<span class='line-break'> </span>which motion under the rule went over to<span class='line-break'> </span>the next meeting.</p>

<div id="page-1134237">
<h3><a name="page-1134237">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 175)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>175</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Finance Committee on settlement with late Treasr &amp; transfer to present Treasr '> Report of Finance Committee on settlement with late Treas<sup>r</sup> &amp; transfer to present Treas<sup>r</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The following as the Report of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee of Finance, was read, accepted<span class='line-break'> </span>and ordered to be recorded. _</p>
<p>"The Committee of Finance, who, by vote<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Trustees on the <date when='1868-05-12'>12<sup>th</sup> of May</date> last, were</p>
<p>'requested to audit the accounts of the [then]<span class='line-break'> </span>present Treasurer to the <date when='1868-06-1'>1<sup>st</sup> of June</date>, and to de<span class='line-break'></span>liver to his successor, upon receiving a satisfactory<span class='line-break'> </span>bond, all books, papers, funds and other<span class='line-break'> </span>property of this Corporation which may be in<span class='line-break'> </span>his possession, giving and taking proper re<span class='line-break'></span>ceipts therefor, and report to the Trustees'</p>
<p>ask leave to Report: _</p>
<p>That they have<span class='line-break'> </span>examined the books of the late Treasurer, and<span class='line-break'> </span>found that the receipts and payments of cash<span class='line-break'> </span>were correctly cast, and satisfactorily vouched: _<span class='line-break'> </span>that the balance of cash in his hands belonging<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Corporation on general account was seventeen<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred eighty four and 51/100 dollars ($1784.51) and,<span class='line-break'> </span>under the Repair Fund, twenty eight hundred and<span class='line-break'> </span>forty and 43/100 dollars, ($2,840.43): _</p>
<p>The Committee also examined the evidences of<span class='line-break'> </span>property of the Corporation and found that the same<span class='line-break'> </span>exhibits as belonging to the Corporation on general account,<span class='line-break'> </span>forty seven thousand nine hundred and fifty dollars,<span class='line-break'> </span>($47,950.00) and, under the Repair Fund, forty two<span class='line-break'> </span>thousand four hundred seventy two and 50/100 dollars, ($42,472.50),<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134238">
<h3><a name="page-1134238">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 176)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>176</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' July 14, 1868 _'><date when='1868-07-14'> July 14, 1868</date> _</span><span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Finance Committee continued _'> Report of Finance Committee continued _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>the details of which are respectively set forth<span class='line-break'> </span>in the schedule A. hereto annexed. _</p>
<p>The aggregate amount of deposit in trust<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Massachusetts Hospital Life Insurance<span class='line-break'> </span>Company, for the Permanent Fund, with the<span class='line-break'> </span>accumulations of Interest, was, on the <date when='1868-01-01'>first day<span class='line-break'> </span>of January 1868</date>, seventy seven thousand nine<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred and seventy nine 26/100 dollars, ($77.979.26),<span class='line-break'> </span>Sixty thousand and twenty three 17/100 dollars being<span class='line-break'> </span>the aggregate of sums deposited, and seventeen<span class='line-break'> </span>thousand nine hundred fifty six 09/100 dollars of<span class='line-break'> </span>accumulations of interest.</p>
<p>A schedule marked B.<span class='line-break'> </span>containing the numbers and dates of the several<span class='line-break'> </span>policies with the several sums deposited, and<span class='line-break'> </span>their respective accumulations of interest, is<span class='line-break'> </span>hereto annexed.</p>
<p>And the Committee gave their receipt<span class='line-break'> </span>to Mr Bond for the aforesaid money and evidences<span class='line-break'> </span>of property, and passed said money and evidences<span class='line-break'> </span>of property to the present Treasurer, taking his<span class='line-break'> </span>receipt therefor. They also received from the Treas<span class='line-break'></span>urer a satisfactory bond for the sum of ten thousand<span class='line-break'> </span>dollars, ($10.000.00).</p>
<p>Deeming it of importance that<span class='line-break'> </span>the United States Bonds, the Certificates of Deposit<span class='line-break'> </span>with the Massachusetts Hospital Life Insurance<span class='line-break'> </span>Company, and other papers of the Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>

<div class="page-content">
<p>177</p>
<p>should be made as secure as possible<span class='line-break'> </span>against loss by fire or robbery, the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>directed the Treasurer to hire a box in the<span class='line-break'> </span>Union Safe Deposit Vaults, which has been<span class='line-break'> </span>done, and the aforesaid evidences of prop<span class='line-break'></span>erty of this Corporation are kept in said vaults.</p>
<p>The Committee have also learned from<span class='line-break'> </span>the late Treasurer, that there is still some amount<span class='line-break'> </span>of money due the Corporation, part of it for bills of long<span class='line-break'> </span>standing: but they are unable to state the aggregate<span class='line-break'> </span>amount with sufficient definiteness to embrace the<span class='line-break'> </span>same in this report. They however annex the accom<span class='line-break'></span>panying communication received from Mr Bond. _</p>

<div id="page-1134241">
<h3><a name="page-1134241">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 179)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>179</p>
<p>[Copy of letter of Geo W<sup>m</sup> Bond, late Treasurer,<span class='line-break'> </span>annexed to the foregoing report.]</p>
<p>"Dear Sir,</p>
<p>I did not know of the adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>meeting to be held tomorrow, if I had, I would have<span class='line-break'> </span>had a more full statement of account ready.</p>
<p>The outstanding accounts on my book amount<span class='line-break'> </span>to about $7400 of which about $2300 are ac<span class='line-break'></span>counts disputed in part or whole, or valueless.<span class='line-break'> </span>Many of these went on the promise of the parties<span class='line-break'> </span>to see Capt. Winsor, and adjust them. This<span class='line-break'> </span>item also includes accounts in your hands<span class='line-break'> </span>in settlement, and valueless accounts, the whole<span class='line-break'> </span>discount on which may be $1000. _</p>
<p>There are many parties I have been unable<span class='line-break'> </span>to find, and cannot judge of the prospect of settle<span class='line-break'></span>ment.</p>
<p>Having now received Capt. Winsor's report<span class='line-break'> </span>can close my book with Mr Barbour and put him<span class='line-break'> </span>in the way of opening his new one so as to<span class='line-break'> </span>show the whole amount outstanding, and make<span class='line-break'> </span>a new move for collection.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Yours Respectfully<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Geo W<sup>m</sup> Bond''</td> </tr> <tr><td>A.J. Coolidge. Esq Treasurer'' </td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

'> <u> <date when='1868-07-14'>July 14, 1868</date>. </u> </span><span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Perpetual Repair of Lots 358 &amp; 359 _ '> Perpetual Repair of Lots 358 &amp; 359 _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary reported that the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on Lots had contracted with W<sup>m</sup> W. Stone proprietor<span class='line-break'> </span>of lot no. 358 and Mrs Elizabeth Stone, widow of<span class='line-break'> </span>Henry B. Stone, late proprietor of lot no. 359, (said<span class='line-break'> </span>lots being contiguous with tombs thereon,) for the per<span class='line-break'></span>petual care of the same, on payment of three<span class='line-break'> </span>hundred and fifty dollars for each lot. _</p>
<p>Voted that said contract be ratified _<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>Adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Attest Austin J. Coolidge Sec.y</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>--------</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ Aug. 11, 1868 '> Trustees _ <date when='1868-08-11'>Aug. 11, 1868</date> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees was<span class='line-break'> </span>held on Tuesday, <date when='1868-08-11'>August 11<sup>th</sup> 1868</date>, at 10 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the President and Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span>Adams, Bowditch, Cheever, Little and Livermore.</p>

Paine Esq<sup>r</sup> addressed to<span class='line-break'> </span>"Dr Jacob Bigelow" upon the subject of the suit of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Granite Railway Company against this Corpor<span class='line-break'></span>ation was read _</p>
<p>Upon which it was</p>
<p>Voted that the Com<sup>ee</sup> on the suit of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Granite Railway Company against this corporation<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<h3><a name="page-1134243">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 181)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>181</p>
<p>(the President &amp; Messrs Rand and Norcross) be <span class='line-break'> </span>instructed to effect a settlement with said Com<span class='line-break'></span>pany on the best terms possible.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Thanks to A. Strauch for gift of Swans _'>Thanks to A. Strauch for gift of Swans _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the thanks of this Board <span class='line-break'> </span>be presented to Mr. A. Strauch of the Spring Grove<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery, Cincinnati, Ohio, for the gift of a pair <span class='line-break'> </span>of Trumpeter Swans. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Question of Charge in case of 2d interment in Public Lot referred to Comee on Interments'>Question of Charge in case of 2<sup>d</sup> interment in Public Lot referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Interments</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary stated that a custom pre<span class='line-break'></span>vails at the Cemetery of charging persons who have<span class='line-break'> </span>purchased a grave in any of the public lots, in <span class='line-break'> </span>case a second or any subsequent interment is made<span class='line-break'> </span>in the same grave, half the current price of the grave <span class='line-break'> </span>at the time of such interment together with the fees<span class='line-break'> </span>of burial _ at the present time amounting to twelve <span class='line-break'> </span>and a half dollars for land and five dollars <span class='line-break'> </span>interment fee, or seventeen and one half dollars: _</p>
<p>That this Board has never had any action to <span class='line-break'> </span>establish these or any rules other than those pub<span class='line-break'></span>lished in the by-laws, and on the back of interment blanks.</p>
<p>Voted that the subject be referred to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee on Interments to report thereon _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Appropriation for purchase of Wyeth House adopted _'>Appropriation for purchase of Wyeth House adopted _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the appropriation of four thou<span class='line-break'></span>sand dollars moved at the last meeting for the pur<span class='line-break'></span>chase of the Wyeth houses land be hereby confirmed.</p>
<p>Adjourned, Attest Austin J. Coolidge, Secretary.</p>

<p>183</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees _ Octo. 13. 1868.'>Trustees _ <date when='1868-10-13'>Octo. 13. 1868</date>.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The regular monthly meeting of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees was held on Tuesday, <date when='1868-10-13'>October 13, 1868</date>,<span class='line-break'> </span>at 10 o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present, the President, Messrs<span class='line-break'> </span>Austin, Bowditch, Cheever, Livermore, <span class='line-break'> </span>Lovejoy, Norcross, Rand and Read. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was <span class='line-break'> </span>read and approved. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Com. on Intermts asked further time _'>Com. on Interm<sup>ts</sup> asked further time _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Committee on Interments to which <span class='line-break'> </span>was referred the qustion of the expediency of <span class='line-break'> </span>charging any land fee in cases of second interments <span class='line-break'> </span>in the public lots, asked further time.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Superintendt under direction of Com. on Grounds to make extensive Removal of Trees _'>Superintend<sup>t</sup> under direction of Com. on Grounds to make extensive Removal of Trees _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President urged the importance of <span class='line-break'> </span>making an extensive removal of trees in the Cemetery;<span class='line-break'> </span>and on motion by Mr Bowditch the following <span class='line-break'> </span>preamble and vote were adopted: _</p>
<p>"Whereas the <span class='line-break'> </span>growth of trees in Mount Auburn has become <span class='line-break'> </span>'detrimental and inconvenient' to the Cemetery by in<span class='line-break'></span>volving a considerable  part of the same in a dense <span class='line-break'> </span>shade, obstructing the views, excluding the sun in <span class='line-break'> </span>many places and thereby killing the grass and <span class='line-break'> </span>preventing the cultivation of flowers, _ It is</p>
<p>Voted that the Superintendent be instructed,<span class='line-break'> </span>under the direction of the Committee on Grounds,</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134246">
<h3><a name="page-1134246">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 184)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>184</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Octo. 13. 1868.'><date when='1868-10-13'>Octo. 13. 1868</date>.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>to remove without unnecessary delay any num<span class='line-break'></span>ber of trees, or of parts thereof, not exceeding one half <span class='line-break'> </span>of the whole number of trees, for the purpose<span class='line-break'> </span>of abating the detriment and inconvenience now <span class='line-break'> </span>occasioned by said trees."</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Amendt of Vote instructing Comee on suit of Granite Railway Co to settle _'>Amend<sup>t</sup> of Vote instructing Com<sup>ee</sup> on suit of Granite Railway Co to settle _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the resolution adopted on the <span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1868-08-11'>11<sup>th</sup> of August 1868</date>, instructing the Committee on the suit <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Granite Railway Company against this <span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation to effect a settlement with said <span class='line-break'> </span>Company on the best terms possible _ be so <span class='line-break'> </span>far amended as to empower said Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>to submit the matters  in controversy to reference.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Com. to inquire &amp; report respecting purchase of land west of Cem.y _'>Com. to inquire &amp; report respecting purchase of land west of Cem.y _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that Messrs Little and Norcross be <span class='line-break'> </span>authorized to inquire and report upon what terms <span class='line-break'> </span>the lot of land westerly of and adjoining the Cemetery <span class='line-break'> </span>now held by the Roman Catholic Bishop can be <span class='line-break'> </span>purchased. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Appropriation towards grading of Coolidge Ave.'>Appropriation towards grading of Coolidge Av<sup>e</sup>.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Cheever having made a statement to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Board that the City of Cambridge contemplate the improve<span class='line-break'></span>ment of the grade of Coolidge Avenue  ~ it was</p>
<p>Voted that Messrs Cheever and Norcross<span class='line-break'> </span>be a Committee to arrange with the City of Cambridge <span class='line-break'> </span>for the payment of two hundred and fifty dollars <span class='line-break'> </span>($250.00 by this Corporation _ when said grading shall <span class='line-break'> </span>have been completed to the satisfaction of this Committee.</p>

<div id="page-1134248">
<h3><a name="page-1134248">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 186)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>186</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Trustees _ Nov. 10. 1868'>Trustees _ <date when='1868-11-10'>Nov. 10. 1868</date></span><span class='line-break'> </span><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report recommitted _'>Report recommitted _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>After discussion it was</p>
<p>Voted that the report <span class='line-break'> </span>be recommitted with instruction to ascertain whether<span class='line-break'> </span>the town of Watertown will permit the use of said <span class='line-break'> </span>ground for burial purposes, and whether the <span class='line-break'> </span>Horticultural Society will join in said pur<span class='line-break'></span>chase, and any other points pertinent to the matter.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Horticultural Soc.y _ its ¼ of Expenses of filling land _'>Horticultural Soc.y _ its ¼ of Expenses of filling land _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the same Committee be requested to <span class='line-break'> </span>ascertain whether the Horticultural Society has been <span class='line-break'> </span>charged with its one quarter proportion of the expenses<span class='line-break'> </span>of improving unsaleable land under the contract <span class='line-break'> </span>with it, especially including the region of Mound <span class='line-break'> </span>Avenue and Halcyon Lake. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Mr Austin added to Com _'>Mr Austin added to Com _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that Mr Austin be added to the <span class='line-break'> </span>Committtee.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Proposal of mayor of Camb. to purchase strip of land from Stone Meadow _'>Proposal of mayor of Camb. to purchase strip of land from Stone Meadow _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>A communication from the Mayor of Cambridge <span class='line-break'> </span>who is Chairman of the Commissioners of the Cambridge<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery, inquiring whether this Corporation will sell the <span class='line-break'> </span>City of Cambridge a strip of land from the Stone Meadow <span class='line-break'> </span>lately purchased by this Corporation of fifty or one hundred<span class='line-break'> </span>feet wide next to said Cemetery _ was laid before the Trustees _</p>
<p>And the same was referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee on Grounds. _</p>

<p>The regular monthly meeting of the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span>was held on Tuesday, <date when='1868-12-08'>December 8<sup>th</sup></date> at 10 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m.</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134251">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 189)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>189</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was read.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Comee relating to purchase of land westerly of Cemetery discharged _ '> Com<sup>ee</sup> relating to purchase of land westerly of Cemetery discharged _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Norcross for the Special Committee to<span class='line-break'> </span>inquire and report on questions connected with<span class='line-break'> </span>the purchase of land westerly of and adjoining the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery, made a verbal statement.</p>
<p>After discussion it was</p>
<p>Voted that the Com<span class='line-break'></span>mittee be discharged so far as relates to inquiries<span class='line-break'> </span>respecting the purchase of the lot westerly of the Cemetery.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Com. to confer with Mass. Hort. Soc.y authorized to secure modifica-tion of Existing contract _'> Com. to confer with Mass. Hort. Soc.y authorized to secure modifica-tion of Existing contract _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Committee associated in relation to the<span class='line-break'> </span>accounts with the Horticultural Society for filling<span class='line-break'> </span>and improving unsaleable land in the Cemetery,<span class='line-break'> </span>verbally reported, through Mr Norcross that<span class='line-break'> </span>the Committee had had a conference with a<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee of the Horticultural Society, and a<span class='line-break'> </span>modification of the existing contract which should<span class='line-break'> </span>secure a complete annual settlement was found<span class='line-break'> </span>acceptable to the Committees, and would be proposed<span class='line-break'> </span>to each Corporation.</p>
<p>It was thereupon</p>
<p>Voted that the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee be empowered to confer witht he Horti<span class='line-break'></span>cultural Society, and secure such alteration of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Existing contract as will authorize this Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span>^<sup>to deduct</sup> the cost of filling and improving unsaleable land in<span class='line-break'> </span>each year from the total amount of sales of each year<span class='line-break'> </span>before making the annual payment to that Society.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ Dec. 8, 1868 _ '> Trustees _ <date when='1868-12-08'>Dec. 8, 1868</date> _ </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Motion that it is inexpedient to invite Hort. Soc.y to join in purchase of Stone Meadow laid on table _'> Motion that it is inexpedient to invite Hort. Soc.y to join in purchase of Stone Meadow laid on table _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Norcross inquired the views of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Board touching the expediency of inviting the <span class='line-break'> </span>Horticultural Society to join with their Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span>in the recent purchase of the Stone Meadow,</p>
<p>After discusion,</p>
<p>It was moved by Mr Livermore</p>
<p><del>Voted</del> that it is inexpedient to dispose<span class='line-break'> </span>of any portion of the Stone Meadow. _</p>
<p>and</p>
<p>On motion by Mr Bowditch,</p>
<p>It was voted that<span class='line-break'> </span>that motion lie upon the table.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Sale of land to Camb. Cemetery _ inexpedient to take action now _ '> Sale of land to Camb. Cemetery _ inexpedient to take action now _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President for the Committee on Grounds stated<span class='line-break'> </span>that the lateness of the season rendered it inexpedient for the<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee to examine the Stone Meadow during the winter<span class='line-break'> </span>with a view to sell any portion thereof to the City of<span class='line-break'> </span>Cambridge.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Granite Railway Co.y suit _'> Granite Railway Co.y suit _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Norcross for the Committee on the suit of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Granite Railway Company against the Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span>reported that he had had further interview with the counsel<span class='line-break'> </span>for the Corporation.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Comee have further time _'> Com<sup>ee</sup> have further time _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The subject was discussed, and<span class='line-break'> </span>on motion of Mr Bowditch</p>
<p>Voted that the Committee have fur<span class='line-break'></span>ther time to report _</p>
<p>Voted that Mr Bowditch be added to the Committee.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Contract for Perpetl Repair Lots 799 &amp; 800 _ '> Contract for Perpet<sup>l</sup> Repair Lots 799 &amp; 800 _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary stated that the Committee on<span class='line-break'> </span>Lots had contracted with the Trustees under<span class='line-break'> </span>the will of the late William F. Whitney, prop<sup>r</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>of lots numbered (799 and 800) seven hundred<span class='line-break'> </span>ninety nine and Eight hundred for the perpetual<span class='line-break'> </span>care of said lots on payment of four hun<span class='line-break'></span>dred and fifty dollars.</p>

<p>Said indenture and votes are as follows: _</p>
<p>"An Indenture of two parts, made their <date when='1869-01-01'>first<span class='line-break'> </span>day of January, A.D. Eighteen hundred sixty nine</date>,<span class='line-break'> </span>by and between the Massachusetts Horticultural<span class='line-break'> </span>Society of the first part, and the Proprietors of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery of Mount Auburn of the second<span class='line-break'> </span>part: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' also vote to be adopted by the Trustees _ '> also vote to be adopted by the Trustees _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Whereas, in and by a certain<span class='line-break'> </span>Indenture by and between the parties dated<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1858-12-18'>December 18, A.D. 1858</date>, and recorded with Middle<span class='line-break'></span>sex Deeds, Lib. 870, folio 365, it was among other<span class='line-break'> </span>things provided as follows:</p>
<p>'Fifth. Whenever lands<span class='line-break'> </span>otherwise unsaleable or unfit for purposes of<span class='line-break'> </span>burial shall be filled up and improved,<span class='line-break'> </span>the cost of such filling up and improvement shall<span class='line-break'> </span>first be deducted from the proceeds of sale,<span class='line-break'> </span>of such lands, and the residue only shall<span class='line-break'> </span>be the amount to be accounted for by the said<span class='line-break'> </span>Proprietors, and to be divided between the two<span class='line-break'> </span>Corporations in the manner specified in the<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ Jany. 12, 1869 '> Trustees _ <date when='1869-01-12'>Jany. 12, 1869</date> </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Supplementary Indenture with Mass. Hort. Soc.y continued _'> Supplementary Indenture with Mass. Hort. Soc.y continued _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>second article of this Indenture; Provided<span class='line-break'> </span>however, that the amount of such residue<span class='line-break'> </span>shall never be less than fifty cents per square<span class='line-break'> </span>foot, except that intermediate spaces between<span class='line-break'> </span>lots, when not intended for burial, may be<span class='line-break'> </span>sold for sixteen and two thirds cents per<span class='line-break'> </span>square foot:</p>
<p>And whereas difficulties have<span class='line-break'> </span>arisen in the construction and carrying into<span class='line-break'> </span>effect the provisions of said article as<span class='line-break'> </span>above set forth, and it has been deemed<span class='line-break'> </span>expedient, and for the interests of the parties<span class='line-break'> </span>concerned, that some modification of the<span class='line-break'> </span>said article should be made:</p>
<p>Now<span class='line-break'> </span>therefore, this Indenture witnesseth _</p>
<p>First _ The said parties, in consideration<span class='line-break'> </span>of the premises, hereby mutually agree to and with<span class='line-break'> </span>each other in manner following, namely,<span class='line-break'> </span>that in the future whenever the said Pro<span class='line-break'></span>prietors shall fill up and improve any of<span class='line-break'> </span>the lands in said Cemetery which are now,<span class='line-break'> </span>or may hereafter become unsaleable, or unfit<span class='line-break'> </span>for burial purposes, the cost of such filling up<span class='line-break'> </span>or improvement, during each and every year,<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be deducted from the gross amount of money<span class='line-break'> </span>received from the sale of lands within the said Cem<span class='line-break'></span>etery during the said year: and the balance then<span class='line-break'> </span>remaining after such deduction, shall be the amount<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<p>to be divided between the said Horticultural<span class='line-break'> </span>Society and the said Proprietors in the proportions as<span class='line-break'> </span>provided and set forth in Article second of said<span class='line-break'> </span>original Indenture:</p>
<p>Second _ It is hereby further<span class='line-break'> </span>understood and agreed by and between the<span class='line-break'> </span>said parties, that the settlements heretofore made<span class='line-break'> </span>by and between the said Corporations by their<span class='line-break'> </span>respective measurers are hereby fully ratified,<span class='line-break'> </span>confirmed and established. _</p>
<p>Third: It is<span class='line-break'> </span>further expressly understood and agreed that<span class='line-break'> </span>the said original Indenture is hereby republished<span class='line-break'> </span>and confirmed, excepting only so far as said<span class='line-break'> </span>Article fifth may be varied by the provisions<span class='line-break'> </span>of this Indenture; but nothing herein contained<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be held or construed to change or vary<span class='line-break'> </span>the minimum rate at which land in said<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery are to be valued in settlement, as set<span class='line-break'> </span>further in the last clause of said Article fifth<span class='line-break'> </span>of said original Indenture.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Votes adopted by Mass. Hort. Soc.y authorizing Supplementary agreement with Proprs of Mt. A. '> Votes adopted by Mass. Hort. Soc.y authorizing Supplementary agreement with Prop<sup>rs</sup> of Mt. A. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Executed and delivered<span class='line-break'> </span>in presence of</p>
<p>At the regular quarterly meeting of the Massa<span class='line-break'></span>chusetts Horticultural Society holden <date when='1869-01-02'>January 2<sup>d</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>A.D. 1869</date>, Charles O. Whitmore from the Finance<span class='line-break'> </span>Committee presented a copy of a supplementary<span class='line-break'> </span>indenture with the Proprietors of the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn, dated <date when='1869-01-01'>January 1<sup>st</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>A.D. 1869</date>, changing the provisions of Article<span class='line-break'> </span>fifth of said original Indenture, but other<span class='line-break'></span>wise ratifying and confirming the same</p>
<p>Whereupon it was</p>
<p>Voted that the sub<span class='line-break'></span>ject be referred to the President of this Society<span class='line-break'> </span>with instructions to report upon the expediency<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Society's executing said Indenture as<span class='line-break'> </span>an adjournment of this meeting one week from<span class='line-break'> </span>today.</p>
<p>At the adjournment of the quarterly meeting,<span class='line-break'> </span>holden <date when='1869-01-09'>January 9, 1869</date>, the President having re<span class='line-break'></span>ported that it is for the best interests of this Society<span class='line-break'> </span>to execute the said Indenture with some<span class='line-break'> </span>slight alterations and additions, and the<span class='line-break'> </span>same having presented as amended in a</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Proprietors&apos; Annual meeting _ Feb.y 1, 1869 _ '> Proprietors' Annual meeting _ <date when='1869-02-01'>Feb.y 1, 1869</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mount Auburn Cemetery</p>
<p>The Annual Meeting of the Proprietors of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery of Mount Auburn will be held<span class='line-break'> </span>at the Horticultural Hall, Fremont Street,<span class='line-break'> </span>Boston, on Monday <date when='1869-02-01'>February 1</date><sup>st</sup> at 3½ o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>p.m., to hear the annual reports and choose<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees for the ensuing year.</p>
<p>Austin J. Coolidge Secretary</p>
<p><date when='1869-01-25'>Jany. 25, 1869</date>.</p>
<p>In accordance with the foregoing notification<span class='line-break'> </span>which was published "in one or more of the Boston<span class='line-break'> </span>newspapers seven days at least before the time<span class='line-break'> </span>of meeting," the proprietors met at the time and<span class='line-break'> </span>place therein named. _</p>
<p>A quorum being in attendance, the President,<span class='line-break'> </span>Dr Jacob Bigelow took the chair. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Records _ '> Records _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The call for this meeting and the record of<span class='line-break'> </span>the last annual meeting were read by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Annual Reports _ '> Annual Reports _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Annual Reports in print having been<span class='line-break'> </span>distributed among the members present, on<span class='line-break'> </span>motion by Jeffrey Richardson Esq, it was</p>
<p>Voted that the reading of the Reports be<span class='line-break'> </span>dispensed with. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p>After discussion of the same, said amend<span class='line-break'></span>ments were withdrawn to allow the original<span class='line-break'> </span>mover to embody the whole in a new motion,<span class='line-break'> </span>incorporating said amendments, which he<span class='line-break'> </span>submitted _ as follows, and the same was adopted.</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Subject of Amendt of Charter continued _ '> Subject of Amend<sup>t</sup> of Charter continued _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion by J.M. Wightman Esq. it was</p>
<p>Voted _</p>
<p>That the Trustees be requested to<span class='line-break'> </span>present to the proprietors, as such adjourned<span class='line-break'> </span>Annual Meeting, any further amendment<span class='line-break'> </span>of the Charter which in their judgment may<span class='line-break'> </span>seem necessary and proper. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Printing &amp; dis-tributing previous Annual Reports _ '> Printing &amp; dis-tributing previous Annual Reports _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion by Lucius R. Paige Esq, it was</p>
<p>Voted that the Trustees be requested to con<span class='line-break'></span>sider the expediency of printing and distributing<span class='line-break'> </span>to the proprietors all the Annual Reports here<span class='line-break'></span>tofore made.</p>

<div id="page-1134270">
<h3><a name="page-1134270">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 208)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>208</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Feby. 1, 1869 _ '> <date when='1869-02-01'>Feby. 1, 1869</date> _ </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees&apos; Annual Report _ '> Trustees' Annual Report _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span><u> Trustees' Report. </u></p>
<p>Among the occurrences worthy of note in the last years' history<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn, is the purchase of two lots or pieces of land<span class='line-break'> </span>situated on the oustide of the Cemetery, and separated from <span class='line-break'> </span>it by an intervening road. One of these, sometimes called<span class='line-break'> </span>the "Stone Meadow" is situated on the easterly side of<span class='line-break'> </span>Coolidge Avenue, and has been brought of the heirs of Cornelius<span class='line-break'> </span>Stone, at the price of $1000 ~ per acre, the lot containing<span class='line-break'> </span>over five and a half acres, and costing the Corporation $5,543.75.<span class='line-break'> </span>This lot, consisting in part of low or wet land, is to be used<span class='line-break'> </span>as a place of temporary deposit for stone, rubbish and building<span class='line-break'> </span>materials, thereby releasing a more valuable portion of land<span class='line-break'> </span>now used for the same purposes within the Cemetery. It is <span class='line-break'> </span>possible that, at some future time, the engine house with its<span class='line-break'> </span>appurtenances may be removed in the same direction, with<span class='line-break'> </span>the same economical purpose. The other purchase is that of a<span class='line-break'> </span>part of an acre of land, with a dwelling house thereon, situated<span class='line-break'> </span>nearly opposite the front gate of the Cemetery, and bought<span class='line-break'> </span>of A. M<sup>c</sup>Donald, for $4,000 ~. For various reasons, it was<span class='line-break'> </span>thought desirable that the Corporation should control this<span class='line-break'> </span>estate.</p>
<p>The work of reclaiming low lands in eligible situations has<span class='line-break'> </span>gone steadily forward. The entire hill on which the<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent's house stood, thirteen years ago, has been<span class='line-break'> </span>levelled, and the earth used to fill up the meadow about<span class='line-break'> </span>Halcyon Lake, and also to restore the necessary grade<span class='line-break'> </span>where made lands have settled, as in some parts of the Lawn,<span class='line-break'> </span>and of the meadow adjoining Thistle Path.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134271">
<h3><a name="page-1134271">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 209)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>209</p>
<p>Considerable sums have been expended in completing the _<span class='line-break'> </span>improvements in S<sup>t</sup> Paul's lot, Central Avenue, and the<span class='line-break'> </span>bank north of the Chapel. As the expense of these necessary<span class='line-break'> </span>improvements within the Cemetery has been shared by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Horticultural Society, an exact account of the sums expended<span class='line-break'> </span>for such purposes, has been rendered to them, and, with a<span class='line-break'> </span>view to prevent any future misapprehension, a new indenture<span class='line-break'> </span>of two parts has been sigend and executed by the authorized<span class='line-break'> </span>agents of the two parties.</p>
<p>A decided progress has been made this winter in removing<span class='line-break'> </span>the superfluous trees and branches from the Cemetery. About<span class='line-break'> </span>one hundred and seventy five cords of wood have already<span class='line-break'> </span>been piled for sale, and much more will be removed during the<span class='line-break'> </span>winter. A marked improvement is already obvious in the<span class='line-break'> </span>variety of the landscape, the extent of the prospect, and the<span class='line-break'> </span>admission of sunlight to the ground. The work of this removal<span class='line-break'> </span>is slow and laborious, owing to the necessity of taking down<span class='line-break'> </span>the trees piecemeal, to avoid danger to neighboring monuments<span class='line-break'> </span>and works of art.</p>
<p>A new border of increased size has been procured for the<span class='line-break'> </span>steam engine, and, for its accommodation, an addition has<span class='line-break'> </span>been made to the engine house, the whole at a cost of about<span class='line-break'> </span>eleven hundred dollars.</p>
<p>A lease having been taken by the Corporation, of rooms at N<sup>o</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>16 Pemberton Square, in Boston, for ten years, it was<span class='line-break'> </span>decided by the Trustees to place the offices of the Secretary<span class='line-break'> </span>and Treasurer in the same building. At this time George<span class='line-break'> </span>W. Bond Esq who has acceptably filled the office of Treasurer<span class='line-break'> </span>for twenty six years, resigned that office, and the Trustees<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134272">
<h3><a name="page-1134272">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 210)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>210</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Feby. 1, 1869 _ '> <date when='1869-02-01'>Feby. 1, 1869</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>subsequently elected Austin J. Coolidge. Esq, to fill both<span class='line-break'> </span>offices of Secretary and Treasurer, a condensation of duties,<span class='line-break'> </span>which, it is hoped, will prove economical to the Corporation,<span class='line-break'> </span>and convenient to the proprietors.</p>
<p>By the Treasurer's Report, it appears that the Permanent<span class='line-break'> </span>Fund, for the future support and preservation of the Cemetery,<span class='line-break'> </span>has increased to $89,818.13. The Repair Fund is now<span class='line-break'> </span>$49,836.24; and the estimated balance in cash and invested<span class='line-break'> </span>disposable property is $48,626.65, exclusive of the real estate<span class='line-break'> </span>owned by the Corporation outside of the Cemetery.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>For the Trustees.<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>(signed). Jacob Bigelow. <u>President</u></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <span class='line-break'> </span>--------------------------</p>

<p>216</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Feby. 1, 1869 _ '> <date when='1869-02-01'>Feby. 1, 1869</date> _ </span></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Treasurer&apos;s Annual Report _ '> Treasurer's Annual Report _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span><u>Treasurer's Annual Report Continued </u></p>
<p>This certifies that I have examined the books and<span class='line-break'> </span>accounts of the Treasurer of the Proprietors of the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>of Mount Auburn for the year Eighteen hundred and<span class='line-break'> </span>sixty eight, and have found them correctly kept &amp; properly<span class='line-break'> </span>balanced, with satisfactory vouchers for all payments charged.</p>
<p>The Certificates of Stocks and other evidences of<span class='line-break'> </span>property were found in accordance with the statements of<span class='line-break'> </span>his accounts.</p>
<p>In the General Account, there appears to be a<span class='line-break'> </span>balance in the hands of the Treasurer of $4,148.55 and <span class='line-break'> </span>in the Fund for Repairs of $2,914.99.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>(signed)</th> <th>Charles C. Little.<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>___</td> <td>Chairman of Finance Committee</td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>

<p><u>Trustees' Records. 1869-70</u></p>
<p>The first meeting of the Trustees for organization and<span class='line-break'> </span>business, was held on Saturday <date when='1869-02-06'>February 6<sup>th</sup> 1869</date> at 10 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m.</p>
<p>There were present Mess<sup>rs</sup> Adams, Austin, Bigelow,<span class='line-break'> </span>Bowditch, Little, Lovejoy, Norcross and Read.</p>
<p>D<sup>r</sup> Bigelow took the chair.</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting of the Trustees and of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Annual Meeting of the Proprietors was read.</p>
<p>The Board proceeded to the choice of officers &amp;  Committees<span class='line-break'> </span>by ballot.</p>
