<div id="page-1134357">
<h3><a name="page-1134357">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 295)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>295</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustee&apos;s Annual Report. '> Trustee's Annual Report. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>the light and the general features of the landscape.</p>
<p>The gale of <date when='1869-09-08'>September 8</date> broke or blew down a considerable<span class='line-break'> </span>number of trees, but did little damage to fences and mon<span class='line-break'></span>uments. A large importation of ornamental flowering shrubs<span class='line-break'> </span>and small trees, ordered last year; has been safely planted<span class='line-break'> </span>in various parts of the Cemetery.</p>
<p>A reception house has been commenced on the Wyeth<span class='line-break'> </span>estate, opposite the front gate of Mount Auburn, for the <span class='line-break'> </span>accommodation and shelter of visitors, and with a cellar<span class='line-break'> </span>for the protection in winter of tender plants or trees.</p>
<p>A lawsuit, which has been pending for several years<span class='line-break'> </span>between this Corporation and the Granite Railway Company,<span class='line-break'> </span>at Quincy, has been settled by a reference, so that the<span class='line-break'> </span>remainder of the stone is to be delivered, and the Receiving<span class='line-break'> </span>Tomb, which was begun some years ago, may now be<span class='line-break'> </span>completed.</p>
<p>An amendment to Article II of the By-Laws was adopt<span class='line-break'></span>ed <date when='1870-01-11'>January 11, 1870</date>, as follows: The words, "The Trustees for<span class='line-break'> </span>the ensuing year shall be elected by ballot," shall be<span class='line-break'> </span>stricken out, and the following inserted in the same place,<span class='line-break'> </span>"The vacancies in the Board of Trustees caused by death,<span class='line-break'> </span>resignation, or by expiration of the term for which any<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees were elected, shall be filled by ballot."</p>
<p>The following amendment to Article VII has also been pass<span class='line-break'></span>ed: "He (the Superintendent) shall not receive from any<span class='line-break'> </span>proprietor, or contractor for work or materials, any commis<span class='line-break'></span>sion or fees, or any compensation for any service rendered<span class='line-break'> </span>by him, except as hereinafter provided. The Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be allowed to render special services in the laying<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134358">
<h3><a name="page-1134358">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 296)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>296</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustee&apos;s Annual Report. '> Trustee's Annual Report. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>out and ornamentation of any lot, upon the request of the<span class='line-break'> </span>proprietor thereof, such proprietor first obtaining a permit<span class='line-break'> </span>in writing from the Secretary; and the Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be allowed to charge such compensation for the<span class='line-break'> </span>services so rendered as the Committee on lots shall approve<span class='line-break'> </span>and shall once in six months render to the Trustees an<span class='line-break'> </span>account in detail of the sums so received."</p>
<p>By the Treasurer's Report, it appears that the Perma<span class='line-break'></span>nent Fund, for the future, support and preservation of<span class='line-break'> </span>the Cemetery, now amounts to $102,466.97 The Repair<span class='line-break'> </span>Fund is now $61,088.86; and the estimated balance in<span class='line-break'> </span>cash and invested disposable property is $50,916.21, ex<span class='line-break'></span>clusive of the real estate owned by the Corporation<span class='line-break'> </span>outside of the Cemetery.</p>
<p>For the Trustees,<span class='line-break'> </span>(signed) Jacob Bigelow, President.</p>

<h3><a name="page-1134364">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 302)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>302</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ March 15, 1870 _ '> Trustees _ <date when='1870-03-15'>March 15, 1870</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees' Records 1870-1.</p>
<p>The regular meeting of the Trustees for organ<span class='line-break'></span>ization and business was held on Tuesday,<span class='line-break'> </span><date when='1870-03-15'>March 15, 1870</date>, at ten o'clock a.m.</p>
<p>There were present the whole Board:</p>
<p>viz.</p>
<p>Messrs Austin, Bigelow, Bowditch, J. T. Bradlee,<span class='line-break'> </span>N. J. Bradlee, Brewer, Livermore, Lovejoy, Norcross,<span class='line-break'> </span>Rand, Sleeper and Turner. _</p>
<p>Dr Bigelow took the Chair. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting of the Trustees,<span class='line-break'> </span>and of the Annual Meeting of the Proprietors<span class='line-break'> </span>was read.</p>
<p>The Board proceeded to organize by<span class='line-break'> </span>the choice of a President.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' President chosen _'> President chosen _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Livermore was appointed a Committee to<span class='line-break'> </span>to receive and count the votes.</p>
<p>The whole number of ballots cast for President was 11 _<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Necessary for choice</th> <th>___</th> <th>6<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>Dr Jacob Bigelow had</td> <td>8</td> <td>___ </td> </tr> <tr><td>John T. Bradlee " [had]</td> <td>2</td> </tr> <tr><td>&amp; Jacob Sleeper " [had]</td> <td>1</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> and Dr Bigelow was declared chosen Pres<sup>t</sup> _<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Resignation of Gatekeeper _'> Resignation of Gatekeeper _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Choice of a Gatekeeper being next in order,<span class='line-break'> </span>the Secretary read a letter from the Gatekeeper<span class='line-break'> </span>tendering his resignation of said office, desiring that<span class='line-break'> </span>it should take effect on the <date when='1870-04-01'>1<sup>st</sup> of April next.</date> _</p>

<div id="page-1134371">
<h3><a name="page-1134371">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 309)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>309</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees&apos; Specl Meeting _ April 2, 1870 _ '> Trustees' Spec<sup>l</sup> Meeting _ <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>A special meeting of the Trustees, called at<span class='line-break'> </span>the request of five members of the Board, was held<span class='line-break'> </span>on Saturday, <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2<sup>d</sup>, 1870</date>, at half past 3<span class='line-break'> </span>o'clock P.m.</p>
<p>The whole Board was present.</p>
<p>The record of the meeting of March 15<sup>th</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>was read. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Application of Geo. C. Richardson to be reimbursed for expenses on adjoining lot '> Application of Geo. C. Richardson to be reimbursed for expenses on adjoining lot </span><span class='line-break'> </span>A letter from Mr George C. Richardson, the<span class='line-break'> </span>proprietor of lot numbered 1525, asking that the<span class='line-break'> </span>Corporation reimburse him, in whole or in part,<span class='line-break'> </span>for expenses incurred by him on the lot of Mr John<span class='line-break'> </span>Peak, which adjoins his own, and was previously<span class='line-break'> </span>in very bad condition _ on the ground that, under<span class='line-break'> </span>the by-law, the Trustees can authorize the repair<span class='line-break'> </span>of a lot in bad condition, at the Expense of<span class='line-break'> </span>the proprietor _ was read,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Referred to Comee on Grounds _ '> Referred to Com<sup>ee</sup> on Grounds _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Upon which it was</p>
<p>Voted that the applica<span class='line-break'></span>tion of Mr Richardson be referred to the Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>on Grounds with full power. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Memorial to purchase and annex land west of Cemetery _ refd to same Comee '> Memorial to purchase and annex land west of Cemetery _ ref<sup>d</sup> to same Com<sup>ee</sup> </span> <span class='line-break'> </span>A memorial from sundry proprietors of lots<span class='line-break'> </span>in the Cemetery asking that measures may be taken<span class='line-break'> </span>to purchase and annex to the Cemetery the lot of<span class='line-break'> </span>six and a half acres of land west and adjoining the<span class='line-break'> </span>Cemetery _ was also referred to the Committee on Grounds.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134372">
<h3><a name="page-1134372">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 310)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>310</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ April 2, 1870 '> Trustees _ <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date> </span><span class='line-break'> </span><u> Trustees Special Meeting, <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date> _ continued _ </u></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Specl Comee on subject recom-mended by Proprs viz _ By-law relating to Supt _ also choice of Supt '> Report of Spec<sup>l</sup> Com<sup>ee</sup> on subject recom-mended by Prop<sup>rs</sup> viz _ By-law relating to Sup<sup>t</sup> _ also choice of Sup<sup>t</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Norcross, for the Committee to which<span class='line-break'> </span>was referred the recommendations of the Proprietors<span class='line-break'> </span>adopted at the Annual Meeting, read the<span class='line-break'> </span>Report of said Committee, of which the following<span class='line-break'> </span>is a copy: _</p>
<p>"Boston <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date>.<span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>___</th> <th>To the Board of Trustees</th> <th>}<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td>___</td> <td>of Mount Auburn Cemetery.</td> <td>}</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> The Committee to<span class='line-break'> </span>whom was referred the recommendations of the Pro<span class='line-break'></span>prietors made at the last annual meeting, and<span class='line-break'> </span>the papers connected therewith, for investigation<span class='line-break'> </span>and examination, make the following Report.</p>
<p>After careful consideration, they recommend the<span class='line-break'> </span>following amendment to the By-laws: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Amendt of By-law Art. 3. Officers _'> Amend<sup>t</sup> of By-law Art. 3. Officers _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Article 3: Strike out all after the word<span class='line-break'> </span>"Trustee" in the third line of the last clause of said<span class='line-break'> </span>article, as printed on the 20<sup>th</sup> page of the catalogue<span class='line-break'> </span>of the year <date when='1867'>1867</date>, and insert the following: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Compensation _ '> Compensation _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>And<span class='line-break'> </span>neither the Superintendent, Gate Keeper, nor any paid<span class='line-break'> </span>officer or servant of the Corporation shall have<span class='line-break'> </span>any interest in, or receive any compensation<span class='line-break'> </span>whatever, direct or indirect for any work designed<span class='line-break'> </span>for the Cemetery, or for any lot or lots therein,<span class='line-break'> </span>or for materials furnished for the same in any<span class='line-break'> </span>manner whatsoever.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134373">
<h3><a name="page-1134373">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 311)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>311</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Amendt to By-law Art. 7 _ Superintt'> Amend<sup>t</sup> to By-law Art. 7 _ Superint<sup>t</sup></span><span class='line-break'> </span>Article 7: Strike out all after the word<span class='line-break'> </span>'By-laws' as printed on the 26<sup>th</sup> line of the 24<sup>th</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>page of the catalogue of the year <date when='1867'>1867</date>, and also<span class='line-break'> </span>the amendment to said article adopted as per<span class='line-break'> </span>records of the Secretary <date when='1870-01-11'>January <del>11</del> ^18<sup>(see p. 276.)</sup> 1870</date>, and insert<span class='line-break'> </span>the following: _</p>
<p>He shall render special<span class='line-break'> </span>services to any proprietor in the laying out<span class='line-break'> </span>and ornamentation of any lot, upon a re<span class='line-break'></span>quest in writing of the proprietor thereof,<span class='line-break'> </span>and shall charge, on account of the Corpor<span class='line-break'></span>ation, such compensation for said services<span class='line-break'> </span>as the 'Committee on Lots may determine,<span class='line-break'> </span>and render^<sup>with the written request of the proprietor (p. 315.)</sup> a detailed statement of all<span class='line-break'> </span>such services monthly, or oftener, to the Treasurer<span class='line-break'> </span>for collection.</p>
<p>The compensation of the Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>shall be a salary, to the fixed annually by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees, and he shall have the use of a house<span class='line-break'> </span>with the grounds hereto belonging, the use of a<span class='line-break'> </span>horse and vehicle, and the services of one man,<span class='line-break'> </span>at the Expense of the Corporation; and he shall<span class='line-break'> </span>have no other perquisites; and he shall not<span class='line-break'> </span>receive from any proprietor or contractor for work<span class='line-break'> </span>or materials any commission, fee, present,<span class='line-break'> </span>or any compensation whatever, direct or indirect,<span class='line-break'> </span>for any services rendered by him, and nothing<span class='line-break'> </span>contained in any other article of the Bylaws shall be so<span class='line-break'> </span>construed as to conflict with or set aside these restrictions.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134374">
<h3><a name="page-1134374">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 312)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>312</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ April 2, 1870 _ '> Trustees _ <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span><u>Trustees' Special Meeting, <date when='1870-04-02'>April 2, 1870</date> _ continued _ </u></p>
<p>In regard to the recommendations of the<span class='line-break'> </span>Proprietors _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Comee relating to Supt continued _'> Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> relating to Sup<sup>t</sup> continued _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>"That the Trustees be requested to place <span class='line-break'> </span>some other Superintendent in office at Mount<span class='line-break'> </span>Auburn instead of Capt. Winsor " _</p>
<p>The Committee<span class='line-break'> </span>not being able to arrive at a unanimous con<span class='line-break'></span>clusion, and deeming it essential to a correct<span class='line-break'> </span>understanding of the matter that the testimony taken _<span class='line-break'> </span>by them should be carefully examined by the<span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees, it was voted to report the same<span class='line-break'> </span>to the Board for such action as they may deem<span class='line-break'> </span>expedient. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report accepted _ '> Report accepted _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Otis Norcross for the Committee."</p>
<p>On motion by Mr Lovejoy it was</p>
<p>Voted that<span class='line-break'> </span>the report be accepted. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Amendt by Arts 3 &amp; 7 of By-laws moved _ '> Amend<sup>t</sup> by Art<sup>s</sup> 3 &amp; 7 of By-laws moved _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The propositions of amendment to articles three<span class='line-break'> </span>and seven of the By-laws contained in the foregoing<span class='line-break'> </span>report were then moved by Mr Norcross, and under<span class='line-break'> </span>the By-laws lie over to the next meeting.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 25 copies of prospect Amendt ordered _'> 25 copies of prospect Amend<sup>t</sup> ordered _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted to print twenty five copies of said<span class='line-break'> </span>proposed amendments to the by-laws, and distribute<span class='line-break'> </span>among the members of this Board</p>
<p>The testimony referred to in the Report was<span class='line-break'> </span>then read. _  [This sentence was added as an amendation to the minutes of this meeting as described on page 314.]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1134375">
<h3><a name="page-1134375">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 313)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>313</p>
<p>Mr Norcross then offered the following<span class='line-break'> </span>resolution: _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Resolution offered to Exhonorate Superintendt '> Resolution offered to Exhonorate Superintend<sup>t</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted _ That the Board of Trus<span class='line-break'></span>tees, in accordance with the suggestions con<span class='line-break'></span>tained in the Report of a Committee to the Propri<span class='line-break'></span>etors at the Annual Meeting, have made a<span class='line-break'> </span>'full and ^<sup>most</sup> thorough investigation' of the complaints<span class='line-break'> </span>referred to, and find that the evidence in the<span class='line-break'> </span>case fails to sustain the charges against the<span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent impeaching his courtesy and<span class='line-break'> </span>propriety of conduct. _</p>
<p>A discussion at considerable length<span class='line-break'> </span>ensued, pending which Mr Read<span class='line-break'> </span>offered an Amendment to the resolution,<span class='line-break'> </span>which he subsequently whithdrew and the<span class='line-break'> </span>question was ordered to be taken. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Question taken by yeas nays _ '> Question taken by yeas nays _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The yeas and nays were called for _</p>
<p>Upon call</p>
<p>Six gentlemen voted yea _</p>
<p>viz Austin, Bowditch, Livermore, Lovejoy,<span class='line-break'> </span>Norcross and Sleeper,</p>
<p>and five gentlemen voted nay _</p>
<p>viz John T. Bradlee, Nath<sup>l</sup> J. Bradlee, Brewer,<span class='line-break'> </span>Rand and Turner _</p>
<p>and Dr Bigelow declined to vote,</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Supt authorized to employ temporary Gate Keeper '> Sup<sup>t</sup> authorized to employ temporary Gate Keeper </span><span class='line-break'> </span><small>Voted that the Superintendent be authorized to employ a temporary Gatekeeper</small><span class='line-break'> </span><table class='tabular'><thead><span class='line-break'> </span><tr><th>Adjourned to the</th> <th>Attest Austin J. Coolidge Secretary<span class='line-break'> </span></th></tr></thead> <tbody> <tr><td><date when='1870-04-12'> 2<sup>d</sup> Tuesd<sup>y</sup> of April</date></td> <td>___ </td> </tr> </tbody> </table></p>

<h3><a name="page-1134380">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 318)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>318</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees Meeting _ Apr. 12, 1870 _ '> Trustees Meeting _ <date when='1870-04-12'>Apr. 12, 1870</date> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span><u>Trustees, Tuesday, <date when='1870-04-12'>April 12, 1870</date> _ continued _ </u> ===</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 2518 '> 2518 </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Emily L. Rich, of Wakefield, daughter of Elkanah<span class='line-break'> </span>Rich, dec<sup>d</sup> prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 2518;</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 3067 '> 3067 </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Lydia Davis of Boston, widow of James Davis<span class='line-break'> </span>dec<sup>d</sup> prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 3067; _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' 3586 '> 3586 </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Ann R. P. Burroughs of Portsmouth, N. H. widow of<span class='line-break'> </span>Charles Burroughs dec<sup>d</sup> prop<sup>r</sup> of lot numbered 3586.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Secretary withdrew _ J. T. Bradlee Sec. pro tem. '> Secretary withdrew _ J. T. Bradlee Sec. pro tem. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary at this point withdrew<span class='line-break'> </span>from the meeting, and</p>
<p>Mr John T. Bradlee was appointed<span class='line-break'> </span>Secretary pro tempore.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report of Comee to consider expediency of continuing union of offices of Sec.y &amp; Treasr '> Report of Com<sup>ee</sup> to consider expediency of continuing union of offices of Sec.y &amp; Treas<sup>r</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Committee which was chosen on the <date when='1870-03-15'>15<sup>th</sup> of<span class='line-break'> </span>March</date> to consider the expediency of continuing the union<span class='line-break'> </span>of the offices of Treasurer and Secretary in one person<span class='line-break'> </span>and to report thereon to this Board, and also to<span class='line-break'> </span>report the name or names of a suitable person or<span class='line-break'> </span>persons for these offices _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Separation recommended _ '> Separation recommended _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>through Mr Rand submitted their Report _<span class='line-break'> </span>recommending the separation of the two offices, and <span class='line-break'> </span>the appointment of two persons to them.</p>
<p>In relation to the nomination of persons to fill<span class='line-break'> </span>the offices of Secretary and Treasurer, and Gate<span class='line-break'></span>keeper the Committee requested further time.</p>
</div>
</div>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Trustees _ Apr. 25, 1870 '> Trustees _ <date when='1870-04-25'>Apr. 25, 1870</date> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>A Special Meeting of the Trustees was<span class='line-break'> </span>held on Monday <date when='1870-04-25'>April 25, 1870</date>, at ten o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>a.m. _</p>
<p>There were present, the President and<span class='line-break'> </span>Messrs J. T. Bradlee, N. J. Bradlee, Brewer, Liver<span class='line-break'></span>more, Rand, and, (before the close of the meeting)<span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Lovejoy. _</p>
<p>The record of the last meeting was<span class='line-break'> </span>read and approved. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Report on Time for Supt elect to enter on his duties _'> Report on Time for Sup<sup>t</sup> elect to enter on his duties _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The President, for the special committee to<span class='line-break'> </span>arrange the time when Mr Folsom shall assume the<span class='line-break'> </span>duties of his office as Superintendent, reported,</p>
<p>recommending<span class='line-break'> </span>that the retirement of the present Superintendent<span class='line-break'> </span>and the induction of the Superintendent elect take<span class='line-break'> </span>place on the <date when='1870-04-30'>30<sup>th</sup> day of April</date>.</p>
<p>Voted to accept the report, and adopt<span class='line-break'> </span>the recommendation. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Sec.y to notify Supt &amp; Supt elect of time for change of Supts _ '> Sec.y to notify Sup<sup>t</sup> &amp; Sup<sup>t</sup> elect of time for change of Supt<sup>s</sup> _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted that the Secretary be directed to inform<span class='line-break'> </span>the present Superintendent that his services will<span class='line-break'> </span>terminate on the <date when='1870-04-30'>30<sup>th</sup> day of April current</date>, and<span class='line-break'> </span>the Superintendent elect, that his time of service<span class='line-break'> </span>will commence at the close of that day.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title=' Transfer of office of Supt refd to Comee '> Transfer of office of Sup<sup>t</sup> ref<sup>d</sup> to Com<sup>ee</sup> </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion by Mr Turner,</p>

<div id="page-1134387">
<h3><a name="page-1134387">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 325)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>325</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Report of the Committee on Grounds on Surveying in Cemetery. _'>Report of the Committee on Grounds on Surveying in Cemetery. _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Rand for the Committee on Grounds to which <span class='line-break'> </span>was referred the subject of surveying in the Cemetery<span class='line-break'> </span>submitted a written report _ recommending that the <span class='line-break'> </span>Superintendent be authorized to contrct with Messrs <span class='line-break'> </span>Shedd and Sawyer for the work specified in Nos. 1.2.3<span class='line-break'> </span>of their letter of <date when='1870-04-04'>April 4, 1870</date> _ the expenses not to exceed <span class='line-break'> </span>five hundred dollars ($500.)</p>
<p>The work described in said letter being _</p>
<p>1. "Write on your section plans all dimensions, and <span class='line-break'> </span>all necessary diagonal and tie lines of lots which may <span class='line-break'> </span>have been omitted."</p>
<p>2. Plot the survey base lines and stations with their <span class='line-break'> </span>reference points on to one of the lithographed plans <span class='line-break'> </span>of the Cemetery, stating all angles and distances in figures.</p>
<p>3. Make a set of partial section plans showing only <span class='line-break'> </span>the relative positions of the lots to the base lines and <span class='line-break'> </span>stations of our survey." _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='accepted _'>accepted _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted to accept the report and adopt its re<span class='line-break'></span>commendations.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt&apos;s request for copy of Sectional plans _ and to employ surveyor to locate stone monts _ at stations. _ '>Sup<sup>t</sup>'s request for copy of Sectional plans _ and to employ surveyor to locate stone mon<sup>ts</sup> _ at stations. _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Rand further presented the several requests of the <span class='line-break'> </span>Sup<sup>t</sup>. "for authority to have a copy of the book of sectional <span class='line-break'> </span>plans, now in the Secretary's office, made for the use of the Supt.<span class='line-break'> </span>and to be kept at the Cemetery." _</p>
<p>"and for authoritiy to employ a surveyor for the purpose of <span class='line-break'> </span>locating stone monuments or stone pegs at the 'stations,' so called, or <span class='line-break'> </span>principal points of reference used by the surveyors in making their <span class='line-break'> </span><small>maps and in creating new lots" _ the Sup<sup>t</sup> suggesting that the work in each</small><span class='line-break'> </span>case would not exceed $300. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='applications for hiring room in Reception House _'>applications for hiring room in Reception House _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>and, on motion by Mr J. T. Bradlee,</p>

<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Fence on W. side of Reception House to be in part removed _'>Fence on W. side of Reception House to be in part removed _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On Motion of Mr N. J. Bradlee,</p>
<p>Voted that the Sup<sup>t</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>under the direction of the Com<sup>ee</sup> on the Reception building be <span class='line-break'> </span>directed to remove the high fence between the grounds of M<sup>c</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>Donald and the new building just erected by the Corpor<span class='line-break'></span>ation, as far back as the rear line of the new building,<span class='line-break'> </span>and to substitute therefor a slat fence not over four <span class='line-break'> </span>feet high.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Finance Com. authorized to settle accounts of Present Treasr; and to transfer property, books, papers &amp;c to new Treas&apos;r &amp; Sec.y _'>Finance Com. authorized to settle accounts of Present Treas<sup>r</sup>; and to transfer property, books, papers &amp;c to new Treas'r &amp; Sec.y _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr Turner,</p>
<p>Voted that the Finance <span class='line-break'> </span>Committee be authorized to settle the accounts of the present <span class='line-break'> </span>Treasurer and Secretary, and receive from him a trans<span class='line-break'></span>fer of the books, papers and property of the Corporation, <span class='line-break'> </span>and deliver the same to his successors in office upon <span class='line-break'> </span>receiving from them the proper receipts and vouchers, and <span class='line-break'> </span>from the Treasurer elect a satisfactory bond in the <span class='line-break'> </span>sum of ten thousand dollars: _</p>
<p>and further that said Committee be authorized <span class='line-break'> </span>to purchase any furniture or other property <span class='line-break'> </span>which may be needful for the office. _</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1134390">
<h3><a name="page-1134390">Trustees Records, Vol. 4, 1865 (page 328)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>328</p>
<p><u>Trustees, Tuesday,<date when='1870-05-10'> May 10, 1870</date> _ continued _</u></p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Open fence on line of J. C. Gray&apos;s land to be arranged for'>Open fence on line of J. C. Gray's land to be arranged for</span><span class='line-break'> </span>Voted to authorize the Com<sup>ee</sup> on the Reception House <span class='line-break'> </span>to arrange with Mr John C. Gray, for an open partition <span class='line-break'> </span>fence between his premises and the lot on which the <span class='line-break'> </span>Reception building stands. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Supt. may employ temporary clerk _ '>Supt. may employ temporary clerk _ </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr J. T. Bradlee,</p>
<p>Voted that the Sup<sup>t</sup> be <span class='line-break'> </span>authorized to employ for such length of time as the Com<sup>ee</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>on change of Sup<sup>t</sup> may deem necessary, a temporary <span class='line-break'> </span>clerk, who shall also act as draughtsman. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Subject of completion of Receiving Tomb refd to Com. on Grounds.'>Subject of completion of Receiving Tomb ref<sup>d</sup> to Com. on Grounds.</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion by Mr Turner, _</p>
<p>Voted that there be  re<span class='line-break'></span>ferred to the Committee on Grounds the  the question what <span class='line-break'> </span>action shall be taken relating to the completion of <span class='line-break'> </span>the Receiving Tomb, and^<sup>that they</sup> report thereon to the Board of <span class='line-break'> </span>Trustees. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Lots out of Repair _'>Lots out of Repair _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr J. T. Bradlee,</p>
<p>Voted that the <span class='line-break'> </span>Sup<sup>t</sup> be requested to report to the Trustees forthwith a list of all <span class='line-break'> </span>lots out of repair in accordance with the 29<sup>th</sup> article of the <span class='line-break'> </span>By-Laws.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Time of Regular Meetings. 2d Wednes.y in month 3½ P.m. '>Time of Regular Meetings. 2<sup>d</sup> Wednes.y in month 3½ P.m. </span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion of Mr J. T. Bradlee</p>
<p>Voted that the regular <span class='line-break'> </span>meetings of the Trustees be held on the <u>second</u> <u>Wednesday</u> of<span class='line-break'> </span>each month, at half past three o'clock P.m.</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Vote abt. Special meetings reconsidd-'>Vote abt. <u>Special</u> meetings reconsid<sup>d</sup>-</span><span class='line-break'> </span>On motion by Mr Livermore,</p>
<p>Voted that the vote by which all special <span class='line-break'> </span>meetings are to be called only at half past three P.m. be reconsidered. _</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>329</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Contracts for Perp. Repair of Lots 645 and 530 _'>Contracts for Perp. Repair of Lots 645 and 530 _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>The Secretary stated that the Committee on Lots had <span class='line-break'> </span>contracted with Nath<sup>l</sup> Fisher, proprietor of lot numbered<span class='line-break'> </span>645 for the perpetual care of said lot for three hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>and twenty five dollars. _ ($325.)</p>
<p>and, respecting lot numbered 530,</p>
<p>with the Exec<sup>rs</sup> &amp; heirs of Sarah Lee, dec<sup>d</sup><span class='line-break'> </span>for he perpetual care of said lot for five hundred <span class='line-break'> </span>dollars ($500).</p>
<p>Voted that said contracts be sever<span class='line-break'></span>ally ratified. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='application of S. J. Locke to have grade of her lot raised _'>application of S. J. Locke to have grade of her lot raised _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>An application from Mrs Sarah J. Locke, repre<span class='line-break'></span>sentative of lot numbered 280, on Orange Path, <span class='line-break'> </span>that the Corporation would raise the grade of her lot <span class='line-break'> </span>to make the same conform to that of neighboring lots, on the <span class='line-break'> </span>ground that the Corporation had changed the grade <span class='line-break'> </span>since the purchase of said lot _ was read, and referred <span class='line-break'> </span>to the Committee  on Grounds to report what action should <span class='line-break'> </span>be taken thereon. _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Application of Mr G. Brewer for leave to ride into Cem.y on horseback _'>Application of Mr G. Brewer for leave to ride into Cem.y on horseback _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>An application from Mr Gardner Brewer, requesting <span class='line-break'> </span>permission to ride into the Cemetery on horseback was read. _<span class='line-break'> </span>and it was</p>
<p>Voted that the Secretary be instructed to notify <span class='line-break'> </span>Mr Brewer of the existing by law respecting admission on <span class='line-break'> </span>horseback _</p>
<p><span class='depth3' depth='3' title='Revision of By law on Admis-sion on horseback refd to Com. on By laws _'>Revision of By law on Admis-sion on horseback ref<sup>d</sup> to Com. on By laws _</span><span class='line-break'> </span>and that the subject of revision of said by-law <span class='line-break'> </span>be referred to the committee on revision of by-laws.</p>
